        const _d = s => atob(s).split('').map(c => String.fromCharCode(c.charCodeAt(0) ^ 42)).join('');

        function getComputerId() {
            let id = localStorage.getItem('permanentComputerId');
            if (!id) {
                const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
                ctx.textBaseline = 'top'; ctx.font = '14px Arial'; ctx.fillText('mongle-fp', 2, 2);
                const fp = `${navigator.userAgent}_${screen.width}x${screen.height}_${navigator.hardwareConcurrency||0}_${navigator.deviceMemory||0}_${canvas.toDataURL().substring(0,50)}`;
                let hash = 0;
                for (let i = 0; i < fp.length; i++) { const c = fp.charCodeAt(i); hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + c; hash = hash & hash; }
                id = Math.abs(hash).toString(36).substring(0, 8);
                localStorage.setItem('permanentComputerId', id);
            }
            return id;
        }

        let userStats = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('userStats') || '{}');
        // Ensure all fields exist
        const _usd = {totalPlays:0,favCount:0,chatCount:0,speedRuns:0,nightPlays:0,earlyPlays:0,uniqueGames:0,uniqueGamesList:[],sessions:0,backToBack:0,sessionGames:0,sessionGamesList:[],lunchPlays:0,weekendPlays:0,searchCount:0,prankCount:0};
        Object.keys(_usd).forEach(k => { if (userStats[k] === undefined) userStats[k] = _usd[k]; });
        userStats.sessions++;
        userStats.sessionGames = 0; userStats.sessionGamesList = []; // reset per-session
        localStorage.setItem('userStats', JSON.stringify(userStats));
        let lastPlayTime = 0, rapidPlayCount = 0, lastGameId = null;

        function checkAchievements() {
            let newUnlocks = [];
            ACH_DEFS.forEach(ach => {
                if (!achievements.includes(ach.id) && ach.req(userStats)) {
                    achievements.push(ach.id);
                    newUnlocks.push(ach);
                }
            });
            localStorage.setItem('achievements', JSON.stringify(achievements));
            if (newUnlocks.length > 0) {
                let delay = 0;
                newUnlocks.forEach(ach => {
                    setTimeout(() => showAchPopup(ach), delay);
                    delay += 3500;
                });
                renderAchievements();
                if (myID) update(ref(db, `presence/${myID}`), { achievements: achievements.length });
            }
        }

        function showAchPopup(ach) {
            const popup = document.getElementById('achPopup');
            const icon = ach.name.split(' ')[0];
            document.getElementById('achPopupIcon').innerText = icon;
            document.getElementById('achPopupName').innerText = ach.name.substring(icon.length + 1);
            document.getElementById('achPopupDesc').innerText = ach.desc;
            popup.classList.add('show');
            setTimeout(() => popup.classList.remove('show'), 3200);
        }

        function renderAchievements() {
            const list = document.getElementById('achList');
            if (!list) return;
            const total = ACH_DEFS.length;
            const unlocked = achievements.length;
            // Group by category
            const cats = { play: '🎮 Gameplay', explore: '🧭 Explorer', social: '💬 Social', skill: '⚡ Skill', secret: '🔒 Secret', award: '🏅 MONGLE Awards', funny: '😂 Funny Awards' };
            let html = `<div style="padding:8px 0; text-align:center; color:#888; font-size:10px; letter-spacing:1px;">${unlocked} / ${total} UNLOCKED</div>`;
            html += `<div style="padding:0 8px 8px;"><div class="ach-progress"><div class="ach-progress-fill" style="width:${Math.round(unlocked/total*100)}%"></div></div></div>`;
            Object.keys(cats).forEach(cat => {
                const catAchs = ACH_DEFS.filter(a => a.cat === cat);
                html += `<div style="padding:4px 8px; font-size:10px; color:#555; letter-spacing:1px; text-transform:uppercase; border-bottom:1px solid #111; margin-bottom:4px;">${cats[cat]}</div>`;
                html += catAchs.map(ach => {
                    const isUnlocked = achievements.includes(ach.id);
                    const icon = ach.name.split(' ')[0];
                    const name = ach.name.substring(icon.length + 1);
                    if (cat === 'secret' && !isUnlocked) {
                        return `<div class="ach-item locked">
                            <div class="ach-icon" style="filter:grayscale(1);opacity:0.3;">🔒</div>
                            <div class="ach-info">
                                <div class="ach-name" style="color:#333;">???</div>
                                <div class="ach-desc">Secret achievement — keep playing!</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>`;
                    }
                    return `<div class="ach-item ${isUnlocked ? 'unlocked' : 'locked'}">
                        <div class="ach-icon" ${!isUnlocked ? 'style="filter:grayscale(1);opacity:0.3;"' : ''}>${icon}</div>
                        <div class="ach-info">
                            <div class="ach-name" style="${isUnlocked ? '' : 'color:#444;'}">${name}</div>
                            <div class="ach-desc">${ach.desc} ${isUnlocked ? '<span style="color:#ffae00;">✓</span>' : ''}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                }).join('');
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;
        }

        window.toggleAch = () => {
            const el = document.getElementById('achDrawer');
            el.classList.toggle('open');
            renderAchievements();
        };

        // ================================
        // LEADERBOARD
        // ================================
        let currentLBTab = 'plays';
        window.toggleLB = () => {
            const el = document.getElementById('lbDrawer');
            el.classList.toggle('open');
            document.getElementById('notifBubble').style.display = 'none';
            if (el.classList.contains('open')) renderLB(currentLBTab);
        };

        window.switchLBTab = (tab) => {
            currentLBTab = tab;
            document.querySelectorAll('.lb-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
            document.getElementById('lbTab-' + tab).classList.add('active');
            renderLB(tab);
        };

        function renderLB(tab) {
            const content = document.getElementById('lbContent');
            if (!content) return;

            if (tab === 'plays' || tab === 'least') {
                const sorted = Object.entries(playStats).sort((a,b) => tab === 'plays' ? b[1]-a[1] : a[1]-b[1]);
                const top = sorted.slice(0, 15);
                if (top.length === 0) { content.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555; padding:20px; text-align:center;">No play data yet</div>'; return; }
                content.innerHTML = top.map(([gameId, plays], i) => {
                    const game = gameData.find(g => g.id === gameId);
                    const name = game ? game.name : gameId;
                    const rankClass = i === 0 ? 'gold' : i === 1 ? 'silver' : i === 2 ? 'bronze' : '';
                    const rankIcon = i === 0 ? '🥇' : i === 1 ? '🥈' : i === 2 ? '🥉' : (i+1);
                    return `<div class="lb-item">
                        <div class="lb-rank ${rankClass}">${rankIcon}</div>
                        <div class="lb-name">${escapeHtml(name)}</div>
                        <div class="lb-score">${plays}</div>
                        <div class="lb-plays">plays</div>
                    </div>`;
                }).join('');
            } else if (tab === 'popular') {
                const popularGames = gameData.filter(g => {
                    const tags = (gameTags[g.id] || []);
                    return tags.includes('popular') || tags.includes('trending');
                });
                if (popularGames.length === 0) { content.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555; padding:20px; text-align:center;">No popular tags set yet. Use the MONGLE panel to tag games!</div>'; return; }
                content.innerHTML = popularGames.map((g, i) => {
                    const plays = playStats[g.id] || 0;
                    const tags = (gameTags[g.id] || []).map(t => `<span class="card-tag ${t}">${t}</span>`).join('');
                    return `<div class="lb-item">
                        <div class="lb-rank">${i+1}</div>
                        <div class="lb-name">${escapeHtml(g.name)} ${tags}</div>
                        <div class="lb-score">${plays}</div>
                        <div class="lb-plays">plays</div>
                    </div>`;
                }).join('');
            } else if (tab === 'users') {
                onValue(ref(db, 'presence'), snap => {
                    const users = [];
                    snap.forEach(c => { const v = c.val(); if(v) users.push(v); });
                    if (users.length === 0) { content.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555; padding:20px; text-align:center;">No users online</div>'; return; }
                    content.innerHTML = users.sort((a,b) => (b.achievements||0)-(a.achievements||0)).map((u, i) => {
                        const rankClass = i === 0 ? 'gold' : i === 1 ? 'silver' : i === 2 ? 'bronze' : '';
                        return `<div class="lb-item">
                            <div class="lb-rank ${rankClass}">${i+1}</div>
                            <div class="lb-name">${escapeHtml(u.name||'?')}</div>
                            <div class="lb-score">${u.achievements||0}</div>
                            <div class="lb-plays">achievements</div>
                        </div>`;
                    }).join('');
                }, { onlyOnce: true });
            }
        }

        // ================================
        // CHAT
        // ================================
        window.toggleChat = () => {
            const el = document.getElementById('chatDrawer');
            el.classList.toggle('open');
            if (el.classList.contains('open')) {
                unreadChat = 0;
                const notif = document.getElementById('chatNotif');
                if (notif) notif.style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('chatInput').focus();
            }
        };

        let chatReplyTo = null;
        let lastChatSent = 0;

        window.sendChat = () => {
            const input = document.getElementById('chatInput');
            const text = input.value.trim();
            if (!text || !myName) return;
            if (text.length > 200) return showToast('Message too long (200 chars max)');
            // Check mute
            if (chatMuted && !isAdmin && !isMongle) return showToast('🔇 Chat is muted');
            // Check if user is individually muted
            if (presenceSnapshot[myID]?.muted && !isAdmin && !isMongle) return showToast('🔇 You are muted');
            // Check slow mode
            if (slowModeSeconds > 0 && !isAdmin && !isMongle) {
                const elapsed = (Date.now() - lastChatSent) / 1000;
                if (elapsed < slowModeSeconds) return showToast(`🐢 Wait ${Math.ceil(slowModeSeconds - elapsed)}s`);
            }
            lastChatSent = Date.now();
            const isAdminMsg = isAdmin || isMongle;
            const msg = {
                name: myName, text, t: Date.now(),
                admin: isAdminMsg, mongle: isMongle
            };
            if (chatReplyTo) { msg.replyTo = chatReplyTo.name; msg.replyText = chatReplyTo.text.substring(0, 60); }
            push(ref(db, 'chat'), msg);
            input.value = '';
            clearReply();
            userStats.chatCount = (userStats.chatCount || 0) + 1;
            localStorage.setItem('userStats', JSON.stringify(userStats));
            checkAchievements();
        };

        window.clearReply = () => {
            chatReplyTo = null;
            document.getElementById('chatReplyPreview').style.display = 'none';
        };

        window.setReply = (name, text) => {
            chatReplyTo = { name, text };
            document.getElementById('chatReplyName').innerText = name;
            document.getElementById('chatReplyText').innerText = text.substring(0, 50);
            document.getElementById('chatReplyPreview').style.display = 'flex';
            document.getElementById('chatInput').focus();
        };

        window.toggleEmojiPicker = () => {
            document.getElementById('emojiPicker').classList.toggle('open');
        };

        window.insertEmoji = (e) => {
            const inp = document.getElementById('chatInput');
            inp.value += e;
            inp.focus();
            document.getElementById('emojiPicker').classList.remove('open');
        };

        window.addReaction = (msgKey, emoji) => {
            if (!myName) return;
            const reactionRef = ref(db, `chatReactions/${msgKey}/${emoji}/${myName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_')}`);
            get(reactionRef).then(s => {
                if (s.exists()) remove(reactionRef);
                else set(reactionRef, true);
            });
        };

        let chatReactions = {};
        onValue(ref(db, 'chatReactions'), snap => {
            chatReactions = snap.val() || {};
            // Re-render reactions in existing messages
            document.querySelectorAll('.chat-msg[data-key]').forEach(el => {
                const key = el.dataset.key;
                const reacts = chatReactions[key] || {};
                let reactEl = el.querySelector('.chat-reactions');
                if (!reactEl) { reactEl = document.createElement('div'); reactEl.className = 'chat-reactions'; el.appendChild(reactEl); }
                reactEl.innerHTML = Object.entries(reacts).map(([emoji, users]) => {
                    const count = Object.keys(users).length;
                    const mine = myName && users[myName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_')];
                    return `<span class="chat-reaction${mine?' mine':''}" onclick="addReaction('${key}','${emoji}')">${emoji} ${count}</span>`;
                }).join('');
            });
        });

        function listenChat() {
            const msgs = document.getElementById('chatMessages');
            let firstLoad = true;
            let lastChatCount = 0;
            let msgKeys = [];
            onValue(ref(db, 'chat'), snap => {
                if (!snap.exists()) { msgs.innerHTML = '<div class="chat-msg system"><span class="chat-name">SYSTEM</span>No messages yet — say something!</div>'; return; }
                const allMsgs = [];
                snap.forEach(c => allMsgs.push({ key: c.key, ...c.val() }));
                // Feed new messages to activity log
                if (!firstLoad && allMsgs.length > lastChatCount) {
                    allMsgs.slice(lastChatCount).forEach(m => { if (m.name && m.text) feedChatMsg(m.name, m.text); });
                }
                lastChatCount = allMsgs.length;
                msgKeys = allMsgs.map(m => m.key);
                const recent = allMsgs.slice(-100);
                const wasBottom = msgs.scrollHeight - msgs.scrollTop - msgs.clientHeight < 40;
                msgs.innerHTML = recent.map(m => {
                    const isMine = m.name === myName;
                    const cls = m.mongle ? 'mongle-msg' : (m.admin ? 'admin' : '');
                    const nameColor = m.mongle ? '#00ffff' : (m.admin ? '#ffae00' : 'var(--primary)');
                    const prefix = m.mongle ? '⚡' : (m.admin ? '🛡️' : '');
                    const time = m.t ? new Date(m.t).toLocaleTimeString([], {hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'}) : '';
                    const reacts = chatReactions[m.key] || {};
                    const reactHtml = Object.entries(reacts).map(([emoji, users]) => {
                        const count = Object.keys(users).length;
                        const mine = myName && users[myName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_')];
                        return `<span class="chat-reaction${mine?' mine':''}" onclick="addReaction('${m.key}','${emoji}')">${emoji} ${count}</span>`;
                    }).join('');
                    const replyHtml = m.replyTo ? `<div class="chat-reply-bar">↩ ${escapeHtml(m.replyTo)}: ${escapeHtml((m.replyText||'').substring(0,50))}</div>` : '';
                    return `<div class="chat-msg ${cls}" data-key="${m.key}">
                        <div class="chat-actions">
                            <span class="chat-action-btn" onclick="addReaction('${m.key}','👍')">👍</span>
                            <span class="chat-action-btn" onclick="addReaction('${m.key}','😂')">😂</span>
                            <span class="chat-action-btn" onclick="addReaction('${m.key}','🔥')">🔥</span>
                            <span class="chat-action-btn" onclick="setReply('${escapeAttr(m.name||'?')}','${escapeAttr(m.text||'')}')">↩</span>
                        </div>
                        ${replyHtml}
                        <span class="chat-name" style="color:${nameColor}">${prefix}${escapeHtml(m.name||'?')}</span>${escapeHtml(m.text||'')}<span class="chat-time">${time}</span>
                        ${reactHtml ? `<div class="chat-reactions">${reactHtml}</div>` : ''}
                    </div>`;
                }).join('');
                if (wasBottom || !firstLoad) msgs.scrollTop = msgs.scrollHeight;

                // Online count in header
                const onlineEl = document.getElementById('chatOnlineCount');
                if (onlineEl) {
                    let c = 0; Object.keys(presenceSnapshot).forEach(() => c++);
                    onlineEl.innerText = c + ' online';
                }

                if (!firstLoad) {
                    const drawer = document.getElementById('chatDrawer');
                    if (!drawer.classList.contains('open')) {
                        unreadChat++;
                        const notif = document.getElementById('chatNotif');
                        if (notif) { notif.style.display = 'flex'; notif.innerText = unreadChat > 9 ? '9+' : unreadChat; }
                    }
                }
                firstLoad = false;
            });
        }

        // ================================
        // GAME TAGS
        // ================================
        // Custom tag definitions: { id, emoji, name, color }
        let customTagDefs = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('customTagDefs') || '[]');

        function syncCustomTagDefs() {
            localStorage.setItem('customTagDefs', JSON.stringify(customTagDefs));
            set(ref(db, 'customTagDefs'), customTagDefs.length > 0 ? customTagDefs : null);
        }

        function listenCustomTagDefs() {
            onValue(ref(db, 'customTagDefs'), snap => {
                if (snap.exists()) {
                    customTagDefs = snap.val() || [];
                    localStorage.setItem('customTagDefs', JSON.stringify(customTagDefs));
                }
                renderCustomTagPills();
                renderCustomTagList();
                if (document.getElementById('tagGameSelect')?.value) renderCustomTagCheckboxes();
            });
        }

        function renderCustomTagPills() {
            const filters = document.getElementById('tagFilters');
            if (!filters) return;
            // Remove old custom pills
            filters.querySelectorAll('.tag-pill.tag-custom').forEach(p => p.remove());
            // Add new ones
            customTagDefs.forEach(ct => {
                const pill = document.createElement('div');
                pill.className = 'tag-pill tag-custom';
                pill.dataset.tag = ct.id;
                pill.style.borderColor = ct.color;
                pill.style.color = ct.color;
                pill.textContent = `${ct.emoji} ${ct.name}`;
                pill.onclick = () => setTagFilter(ct.id);
                if (activeTagFilter === ct.id) { pill.classList.add('active'); pill.style.background = ct.color; pill.style.color = '#000'; }
                filters.appendChild(pill);
            });
        }

        function renderCustomTagList() {
            const el = document.getElementById('customTagList');
            if (!el) return;
            if (customTagDefs.length === 0) { el.innerHTML = '<span style="color:#333; font-size:10px;">No custom tags yet</span>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = customTagDefs.map(ct => `
                <div class="custom-tag-badge" style="border-color:${ct.color}; color:${ct.color};">
                    ${ct.emoji} ${escapeHtml(ct.name)}
                    <button onclick="deleteCustomTag('${ct.id}')" title="Delete tag">✕</button>
                </div>`).join('');
        }

        function renderCustomTagCheckboxes() {
            const el = document.getElementById('customTagCheckboxes');
            if (!el) return;
            const gameId = document.getElementById('tagGameSelect')?.value;
            const currentTags = gameTags[gameId] || [];
            if (customTagDefs.length === 0) { el.innerHTML = '<span style="color:#333; font-size:10px;">No custom tags created yet</span>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = customTagDefs.map(ct => `
                <label style="font-size:11px; display:flex; align-items:center; gap:4px; color:${ct.color};">
                    <input type="checkbox" data-ctag="${ct.id}" ${currentTags.includes(ct.id) ? 'checked' : ''}> ${ct.emoji} ${escapeHtml(ct.name)}
                </label>`).join('');
        }

        window.createCustomTag = () => {
            if (!isMongle) return alert('MONGLE access required.');
            const emoji = document.getElementById('newTagEmoji').value.trim() || '🏷️';
            const name = document.getElementById('newTagName').value.trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,'_');
            const color = document.getElementById('newTagColor').value || '#00ff41';
            if (!name) return alert('Enter a tag name.');
            if (name.length > 20) return alert('Tag name too long (20 chars max).');
            const id = 'ct_' + name;
            if (customTagDefs.find(t => t.id === id)) return alert('That tag already exists.');
            customTagDefs.push({ id, emoji, name: name.replace(/_/g,' '), color });
            syncCustomTagDefs();
            document.getElementById('newTagEmoji').value = '';
            document.getElementById('newTagName').value = '';
            renderCustomTagPills();
            renderCustomTagList();
            renderCustomTagCheckboxes();
            showToast(`Tag "${emoji} ${name}" created!`);
        };

        window.deleteCustomTag = (id) => {
            if (!isMongle) return alert('MONGLE access required.');
            if (!confirm(`Delete this tag? It will be removed from all games.`)) return;
            customTagDefs = customTagDefs.filter(t => t.id !== id);
            // Remove from all games
            Object.keys(gameTags).forEach(gid => {
                gameTags[gid] = gameTags[gid].filter(t => t !== id);
                set(ref(db, `gameTags/${gid}`), gameTags[gid].length > 0 ? gameTags[gid] : null);
            });
            syncCustomTagDefs();
            renderCustomTagPills();
            renderCustomTagList();
            renderCustomTagCheckboxes();
            renderGrid();
            showToast('Tag deleted.');
        };

        window.setTagFilter = (tag) => {
            activeTagFilter = tag;
            document.querySelectorAll('.tag-pill').forEach(p => {
                const isActive = p.dataset.tag === tag;
                p.classList.toggle('active', isActive);
                // Handle custom tag active color
                const ct = customTagDefs.find(c => c.id === p.dataset.tag);
                if (ct) {
                    if (isActive) { p.style.background = ct.color; p.style.color = '#000'; }
                    else { p.style.background = ''; p.style.color = ct.color; }
                }
            });
            renderGrid();
        };
        document.querySelector('[data-tag="all"]').classList.add('active');

        // Populate tag game select
        function populateTagSelect() {
            const sel = document.getElementById('tagGameSelect');
            if (!sel || gameData.length === 0) return;
            sel.innerHTML = gameData.map(g => `<option value="${g.id}">${escapeHtml(g.name)}</option>`).join('');
            sel.onchange = () => {
                const tags = gameTags[sel.value] || [];
                document.getElementById('tgPopular').checked = tags.includes('popular');
                document.getElementById('tgTrending').checked = tags.includes('trending');
                document.getElementById('tgMulti').checked = tags.includes('multiplayer');
                document.getElementById('tgNoLag').checked = tags.includes('nolag');
                document.getElementById('tgNew').checked = tags.includes('new');
                renderCustomTagCheckboxes();
            };
            sel.dispatchEvent(new Event('change'));
            renderCustomTagList();
        }

        window.saveGameTags = () => {
            if (!isMongle) return alert('MONGLE access required.');
            const sel = document.getElementById('tagGameSelect');
            const gameId = sel.value;
            const tags = [];
            if (document.getElementById('tgPopular').checked) tags.push('popular');
            if (document.getElementById('tgTrending').checked) tags.push('trending');
            if (document.getElementById('tgMulti').checked) tags.push('multiplayer');
            if (document.getElementById('tgNoLag').checked) tags.push('nolag');
            if (document.getElementById('tgNew').checked) tags.push('new');
            // Add checked custom tags
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-ctag]:checked').forEach(cb => tags.push(cb.dataset.ctag));
            gameTags[gameId] = tags;
            localStorage.setItem('gameTags', JSON.stringify(gameTags));
            set(ref(db, `gameTags/${gameId}`), tags.length > 0 ? tags : null);
            showToast('Tags saved!');
            renderGrid();
        };

        // Listen for global game tags from firebase
        function listenGameTags() {
            onValue(ref(db, 'gameTags'), snap => {
                if (!snap.exists()) return;
                snap.forEach(c => {
                    if (c.val()) gameTags[c.key] = c.val();
                    else delete gameTags[c.key];
                });
                localStorage.setItem('gameTags', JSON.stringify(gameTags));
                renderGrid();
            });
        }

        // ================================
        // GAME STATS
        // ================================
        window.showGameStats = (mode) => {
            const el = document.getElementById('gameStatsList');
            const sorted = Object.entries(playStats).sort((a,b) => mode === 'top' ? b[1]-a[1] : a[1]-b[1]).slice(0, 10);
            const max = sorted[0] ? sorted[0][1] : 1;
            if (sorted.length === 0) { el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555; padding:10px; font-size:11px;">No play data yet</div>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = sorted.map(([gameId, plays]) => {
                const game = gameData.find(g => g.id === gameId);
                const name = game ? game.name : gameId;
                const pct = Math.round((plays / max) * 100);
                return `<div class="game-stat-row">
                    <div class="game-stat-name">${escapeHtml(name.substring(0,20))}</div>
                    <div class="game-stat-bar"><div class="game-stat-fill" style="width:${pct}%"></div></div>
                    <div class="game-stat-plays">${plays}</div>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        };

        // ================================
        // SECRET ACHIEVEMENT HELPER
        // ================================
        function awardSecretAch(id) {
            if (achievements.includes(id)) return;
            const ach = ACH_DEFS.find(a => a.id === id);
            if (!ach) return;
            achievements.push(id);
            localStorage.setItem('achievements', JSON.stringify(achievements));
            setTimeout(() => { showAchPopup(ach); renderAchievements(); if(myID) update(ref(db,`presence/${myID}`), {achievements: achievements.length}); }, 1500);
        }

        // ================================
        // GAME TAB MONITOR (admin side)
        // ================================
        function startGameTabMonitor() {
            onValue(ref(db,'presence'), snap => {
                const list = document.getElementById('gameTabList');
                const sel = document.getElementById('gameTabUserSel');
                const countEl = document.getElementById('gameTabCount');
                if (!list) return;
                const active = [];
                snap.forEach(c => {
                    const v = c.val() || {};
                    if (v.activeGame) active.push({key: c.key, ...v});
                });
                countEl.innerText = `(${active.length} active)`;
                if (active.length === 0) {
                    list.innerHTML = '<div class="gtab-empty">No users have games open right now.</div>';
                    if (sel) sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- No active game tabs --</option>';
                    return;
                }
                list.innerHTML = active.map(u => {
                    const elapsed = u.gameStarted ? Math.floor((Date.now() - u.gameStarted) / 1000) : 0;
                    const timeStr = elapsed < 60 ? `${elapsed}s` : `${Math.floor(elapsed/60)}m ${elapsed%60}s`;
                    return `<div class="gtab-item">
                        <div>
                            <div class="gtab-name"><span class="gtab-live"></span>${escapeHtml(u.activeGame||'?')}</div>
                            <div class="gtab-user">${escapeHtml(u.name||'?')} — ${timeStr}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="gtab-actions">
                            <button class="btn btn-red" onclick="adminCloseGameFor('${u.key}')" style="padding:3px 7px; font-size:9px;" title="Close game">✖</button>
                            <button class="btn btn-warn" onclick="adminDisableGameFor('${u.key}')" style="padding:3px 7px; font-size:9px;" title="Disable game">🚫</button>
                            <button class="btn btn-dark" onclick="adminGameMsgFor('${u.key}', '${escapeAttr(u.name||'?')}', '${escapeAttr(u.activeGame||'?')}')" style="padding:3px 7px; font-size:9px;" title="Send alert">📢</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                }).join('');
                if (sel) sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select user --</option>' + active.map(u => `<option value="${u.key}">${escapeHtml(u.name||'?')} — ${escapeHtml(u.activeGame||'?')}</option>`).join('');
            });
        }

        window.adminCloseGameFor = (uid) => {
            update(ref(db,`presence/${uid}`), {closeGame: true, activeGame: null, activeGameUrl: null, activeGameId: null, gameStarted: null, activity: 'Browsing'});
            showToast('Game close sent!');
        };
        window.adminDisableGameFor = (uid) => {
            update(ref(db,`presence/${uid}`), {prank: 'disable-game'});
            showToast('Game disabled!');
        };
        window.adminGameMsgFor = (uid, userName, gameName) => {
            const msg = prompt(`Send alert to ${userName} about their game "${gameName}":`);
            if (msg?.trim()) { update(ref(db,`presence/${uid}`), {msg: msg.trim()}); showToast('Alert sent!'); }
        };
        window.adminSelectUser = (uid) => {
            selectedID = uid;
            const val = presenceSnapshot[uid];
            if (val) updateDossier(val, uid);
            document.querySelectorAll('.u-item').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('selected'));
            showToast('User selected in overseer!');
        };
        window.adminCloseGame = () => {
            const sel = document.getElementById('gameTabUserSel');
            if (!sel?.value) return alert('Select a user with game open');
            adminCloseGameFor(sel.value);
        };
        window.adminDisableGame = () => {
            const sel = document.getElementById('gameTabUserSel');
            if (!sel?.value) return alert('Select a user with game open');
            adminDisableGameFor(sel.value);
        };
        window.adminGameMsg = () => {
            const sel = document.getElementById('gameTabUserSel');
            if (!sel?.value) return alert('Select a user with game open');
            const userData = presenceSnapshot[sel.value] || {};
            adminGameMsgFor(sel.value, userData.name||'?', userData.activeGame||'?');
        };

        // ================================
        // ACHIEVEMENT AWARD (MONGLE)
        // ================================
        window.awardAchievement = () => {
            if (!isMongle) return alert('MONGLE access required.');
            const userSel = document.getElementById('awardUserSelect');
            const achSel = document.getElementById('awardAchSelect');
            if (!userSel.value) return alert('Select a user.');
            update(ref(db, `presence/${userSel.value}`), { grantAch: achSel.value });
            showToast('Achievement sent!');
        };

        // ================================
        // SMART AUTO-CATEGORIZER
        // ================================
        function autoCategory(name) {
            const n = name.toLowerCase();
            // Each category has keyword arrays - first match wins
            const cats = [
                ['shooting',    ['shoot','gun','bullet','sniper','fps','warfare','warzone','combat','aim','trigger','pistol','rifle','zombie shoot','counter','strike','valorant','crossfire','krunker','shellshock','war','battle royale','fortnite','pubg','overwatch','apex']],
                ['racing',      ['race','racing','drift','speed','drive','car','vehicle','kart','bike','motorcycle','truck','highway','road','traffic','turbo','nitro','moto','slope','parkour run','dash','sprint','run 3','run 2','temple run','subway','jetpack','skateboard']],
                ['survival',    ['survival','survive','craft','mine','build','sandbox','terraria','minecraft','roblox','among us','impostor','sus','escape','dungeon','roguelike','rouge','permadeath','idle','clicker','cookie','incremental','tycoon','idle miner']],
                ['horror',      ['horror','fnaf','freddy','scary','night','haunted','creepy','ghost','terror','fear','evil','monster','slenderman','granny','piggy','poppy','playtime','huggy','wuggy','bendy','siren head','baldi']],
                ['puzzle',      ['puzzle','logic','brain','think','solve','block','tetris','2048','sudoku','wordle','crossword','match','mahjong','jigsaw','memory','pattern','riddle','escape room','portal','cut the rope','angry birds','physics','connect','merge','sokoban','swap','slide']],
                ['platformer',  ['jump','platform','mario','sonic','run','hop','bounce','leap','metroid','megaman','kirby','donkey kong','celeste','hollow knight','geometry dash','flappy','bird','frog','bunny','cat mario','fireboy','watergirl','stickman','prince','king','hero','adventure','quest']],
                ['io',          ['.io','agar','slither','diep','mope','paper','splix','hole','brutal','spinz','wings','defly','yohoho','zombs','wormate','starve','kirka','surviv','krunker','bloxd','skribbl','gartic','sketchful','drawasaurus']],
                ['sports',      ['football','soccer','basketball','baseball','hockey','tennis','golf','cricket','rugby','volleyball','swim','olympic','sport','nba','nfl','fifa','mlb','madden','2k','skate','ski','snowboard','bmx','boxing','wrestling','mma','fight','punch','kick','ball']],
                ['action',      ['action','fight','battle','attack','warrior','ninja','samurai','knight','sword','blade','axe','spear','bow','arrow','katana','punch','kick','brawl','street fight','mortal','kombat','tekken','smash','beat','hack','slash','dragon','fire','magic','spell','wizard','witch']],
                ['strategy',    ['strategy','tower defense','chess','checkers','card','deck','war','risk','civ','civilization','age of','command','conquer','empire','kingdom','castle','defend','base','siege','troops','army','squad','tactical','rts','turn based','hearthstone','clash']],
                ['rhythm',      ['music','rhythm','dance','beat','song','fnf','friday night','funkin','guitar','piano','drum','dj','concert','sing','karaoke','melody','tune','rap','hip hop','band','rock','pop','jazz']],
                ['simulation',  ['sim','simulate','fly','flight','pilot','plane','helicopter','boat','ship','farm','farming','cooking','chef','restaurant','doctor','surgery','hospital','life','dating','pet','animal','aquarium','zoo','city','town','manage','business']],
                ['casual',      ['casual','click','tap','idle','relax','chill','fun','party','mini','word','quiz','trivia','hangman','uno','ludo','monopoly','snake','pong','pac man','pacman','tetris','candy','bubble','pop','farm','garden','cute','kawaii']],
                ['five nights at freddys', ['fnaf','five nights','freddy','foxy','bonnie','chica','glamrock','security breach','sister location','pizzeria']],
            ];

            for (const [cat, keywords] of cats) {
                if (keywords.some(k => n.includes(k))) return cat;
            }
            return 'other';
        }

        // ================================
        // GITHUB GAME LOADER
        // ================================
        async function loadGithubGames() {
            try {
                const response = await fetch('https://api.github.com/repos/Idonotknowhowtocodeyet/mongles-pull-games/contents/');
                const files = await response.json();
                const fetchedGames = files.filter(f => f.name.endsWith('.html')).map(f => {
                    const name = f.name.replace('.html', '').replace(/-/g, ' ').replace(/_/g, ' ');
                    const displayName = name.replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase());
                    return {
                        id: f.sha,
                        name: displayName,
                       url: `https://raw.githack.com/Idonotknowhowtocodeyet/mongles-pull-games/main/${f.name}`,
                        category: autoCategory(name)
                    };
                });
                gameData = fetchedGames;
                // Auto-apply tags based on category
                const autoTagMap = {
                    'shooting': ['popular'],
                    'io': ['multiplayer'],
                    'sports': ['multiplayer'],
                    'horror': ['popular'],
                    'racing': ['nolag'],
                    'puzzle': ['nolag'],
                    'platformer': ['nolag'],
                    'casual': ['nolag'],
                };
                const savedTags = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('gameTags') || '{}');
                let tagsChanged = false;
                fetchedGames.forEach(g => {
                    const autoTags = autoTagMap[g.category] || [];
                    if (autoTags.length && !savedTags[g.id]) {
                        savedTags[g.id] = autoTags;
                        tagsChanged = true;
                    }
                });
                if (tagsChanged) {
                    localStorage.setItem('gameTags', JSON.stringify(savedTags));
                    gameTags = savedTags;
                    // Sync to Firebase if admin
                    if (isMongle || isAdmin) set(ref(db, 'gameTags'), savedTags);
                }
                renderGrid();
                populateTagSelect();
                console.log("GitHub Games Synced:", gameData.length);
                // Log category breakdown
                const breakdown = {};
                fetchedGames.forEach(g => { breakdown[g.category] = (breakdown[g.category]||0)+1; });
                console.log("Categories:", breakdown);
            } catch (e) { console.error("Sync error:", e); }
        }
        loadGithubGames();

        // ================================
        // BAN CHECK
        // ================================
        function checkBan() {
            onValue(ref(db, `bans/${COMPUTER_ID}`), (snap) => {
                if (snap.exists()) {
                    document.getElementById('bannedDeviceId').innerText = COMPUTER_ID;
                    document.getElementById('banned').style.display = 'block';
                    document.getElementById('lockdown').style.display = 'none';
                    document.getElementById('app').style.display = 'none';
                    document.getElementById('loginOverlay').style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }
        checkBan();

        function trackIdName(id, name) {
            const idLog = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('idLog') || '{}');
            if (!idLog[id]) idLog[id] = [];
            if (!idLog[id].includes(name)) idLog[id].push(name);
            localStorage.setItem('idLog', JSON.stringify(idLog));
            if (isMongle) set(ref(db, `idLog/${id}`), { names: idLog[id], lastSeen: new Date().toISOString() });
        }

        function logError(msg) {
            try {
                const el = document.getElementById('adminErrorLog');
                if (!el) return;
                const entry = document.createElement('div');
                entry.className = 'err-item';
                entry.innerText = `${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()} — ${msg}`;
                if (el.innerText === 'No errors yet.') el.innerHTML = '';
                el.prepend(entry);
                while (el.children.length > 30) el.removeChild(el.lastChild);
            } catch(e){}
        }
        window.clearErrorLog = () => { document.getElementById('adminErrorLog').innerHTML = 'No errors yet.'; };
        window.addEventListener('error', (ev) => logError(ev.message || 'Error'));
        window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', (ev) => logError('Promise: ' + (ev.reason?.message || ev.reason)));

        // ================================
        // PANIC KEY
        // ================================
        const keyDisp = document.getElementById('cfgKeyDisp');
        keyDisp.value = cfg.key.toUpperCase();
        keyDisp.onclick = () => {
            keyDisp.value = "[ PRESS KEY NOW ]"; keyDisp.style.background = "#111";
            const handler = (e) => { e.preventDefault(); tempKey = e.key; keyDisp.value = e.key.toUpperCase(); keyDisp.style.background = "#000"; window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler); };
            window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
        };

        // ================================
        // THEME / CLOAK
        // ================================
        function applyTheme(t) {
            const root = document.documentElement.style;
            // Reset body first
            document.body.style.backgroundImage = 'none';
            document.body.style.backgroundSize = '';
            if (t === 'clever') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#0b63d1'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#f6f9fc'); root.setProperty('--card', '#ffffff');
                root.setProperty('--accent', '#d0e8ff');
                document.body.style.background = '#f6f9fc'; document.body.style.color = '#111';
            } else if (t === 'canva') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#7c5cff'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#0f172a'); root.setProperty('--card', '#1e1b4b');
                document.body.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#0f172a,#1e1b4b)'; document.body.style.color = '#fff';
            } else if (t === 'website') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#2d3748'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#f4f6f8'); root.setProperty('--card', '#fff');
                document.body.style.background = '#f4f6f8'; document.body.style.color = '#111';
            } else if (t === 'halloween') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#ff6b00'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#0d0007'); root.setProperty('--card', '#1a000f');
                root.setProperty('--accent', '#2a0010'); root.setProperty('--glow', '0 0 10px #ff6b0077');
                document.body.style.background = '#0d0007'; document.body.style.color = '#ff6b00';
                document.title = '🎃 ' + document.title.replace(/^[^ ]+ /, '');
            } else if (t === 'christmas') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#00d44b'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#001a08'); root.setProperty('--card', '#002010');
                root.setProperty('--accent', '#002010'); root.setProperty('--err', '#ff2020');
                document.body.style.background = 'linear-gradient(180deg,#001a08,#000d04)'; document.body.style.color = '#00d44b';
            } else if (t === 'aprilfools') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#ff0080'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#0a0015'); root.setProperty('--card', '#100020');
                document.body.style.background = '#0a0015'; document.body.style.color = '#ff0080';
                document.body.style.backgroundImage = 'radial-gradient(circle at 20% 50%, #ff008011, transparent 40%), radial-gradient(circle at 80% 20%, #00ff4111, transparent 40%)';
            } else if (t === 'valentines') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#ff4d8f'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#0d0008'); root.setProperty('--card', '#1a0010');
                root.setProperty('--glow', '0 0 10px #ff4d8f77');
                document.body.style.background = '#0d0008'; document.body.style.color = '#ff4d8f';
            } else if (t === 'cyberpunk') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#ff00ff'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#000010'); root.setProperty('--card', '#0a000f');
                root.setProperty('--blue', '#ff00ff'); root.setProperty('--glow', '0 0 10px #ff00ff77');
                document.body.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#000010,#100005)'; document.body.style.color = '#ff00ff';
                document.body.style.backgroundImage = 'repeating-linear-gradient(0deg,transparent,transparent 40px,#ff00ff08 40px,#ff00ff08 41px)';
            } else if (t === 'retro') {
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#39ff14'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#001000'); root.setProperty('--card', '#002000');
                root.setProperty('--glow', '0 0 10px #39ff1477');
                document.body.style.background = '#001000'; document.body.style.color = '#39ff14';
                document.body.style.backgroundImage = 'radial-gradient(ellipse at center, #003000 0%, #001000 100%)';
            } else {
                // mongle default
                root.setProperty('--primary', '#00ff41'); root.setProperty('--bg', '#000'); root.setProperty('--card', '#0a0a0a');
                root.setProperty('--accent', '#003b00'); root.setProperty('--glow', '0 0 10px #00ff4177');
                document.body.style.background = '#000'; document.body.style.color = '#00ff41';
            }
        }

        // ================================
        // DOORS (admin login)
        // ================================
        window.door = (type) => {
            if (type === 'admin') {
                const code = prompt(_d('a39+YnVpZW5vEA=='));
                if (code === _d('Z2VkbWZvdWtuZ2Nk')) {
                    isAdmin = true;
                    const ab = document.getElementById('adminBtn');
                    ab.style.display = "block";
                    ab.style.opacity = "1";
                    ab.style.position = "relative";
                    ab.style.pointerEvents = "auto";
                    document.getElementById('badge').innerText = "[OVERSEER]";
                    const mongleCode = prompt(_d('Z2VkbWZvCmllbm8KAkVYCklLRElPRgMQ'));
                    if (mongleCode === _d('Z2VkbWZvdWV9ZG94')) {
                        isMongle = true;
                        document.getElementById('mongleBtn').style.display = "block";
                        document.getElementById('badge').innerHTML = '<span class="mongle-badge">[⚡MONGLE⚡]</span>';
                    }
                    const nameField = document.getElementById('username');
                    if (!nameField.value.trim()) nameField.value = isMongle ? 'MONGLE' : 'OVERSEER';
                    initSession();
                } else if (code) { alert("Bad code."); }
            } else {
                document.getElementById('loginOverlay').style.display = 'flex';
                if (isMongle) showLobbyUsers();
            }
        };

        window.closeLogin = () => { document.getElementById('loginOverlay').style.display = 'none'; };

        function showLobbyUsers() {
            if (!isMongle) return;
            document.getElementById('lobbyUsersContainer').style.display = 'block';
            onValue(ref(db, 'lobby'), (snap) => {
                const container = document.getElementById('lobbyUsers');
                container.innerHTML = '';
                if (!snap.exists()) { container.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#444; padding:8px;">No one waiting</div>'; return; }
                snap.forEach(c => {
                    const u = c.val();
                    const div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.className = 'lobby-user';
                    div.innerHTML = `<b>${u.computerId}</b> — ${new Date(u.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString()}`;
                    container.appendChild(div);
                });
            });
        }

        }

        // ================================

        window.initSession = async () => {
            myName = document.getElementById('username').value.trim() || "User_" + Math.floor(Math.random()*9999);
            trackIdName(COMPUTER_ID, myName);
            document.getElementById('lockdown').style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById('loginOverlay').style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById('app').style.display = "flex";
            applyTheme(cfg.theme);
            applyCloak(cfg.cloak);
            updatePanicOptions();
            document.getElementById('cfgUrl').value = cfg.url;
            document.getElementById('cfgKeyDisp').value = cfg.key.toUpperCase();
            document.getElementById('cfgMode').value = cfg.mode;
            document.getElementById('chkEnable').innerText = cfg.enable ? '✓' : '';
            document.getElementById('cfgTheme').value = cfg.theme;
            document.getElementById('cfgCloak').value = cfg.cloak;
            document.getElementById('panicMode').value = cfg.panicMode;

            let ipInfo = { ip: 'Hidden', city: '?', region: '?', org: '?' };
            try { const r = await fetch('https://ipapi.co/json/'); if(r.ok) ipInfo = await r.json(); } catch(e){}
            const bat = await navigator.getBattery?.().catch(() => ({}));

            // Use a per-TAB session ID so same computer can be tested in multiple tabs
            // Real users on different computers will still get one slot each (COMPUTER_ID based)
            const TAB_ID = sessionStorage.getItem('tabId') || (() => { const id = COMPUTER_ID + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6); sessionStorage.setItem('tabId', id); return id; })();
            myID = TAB_ID;
            userRef = ref(db, `presence/${myID}`);
            await set(userRef, {
                name: myName, activity: 'Browsing', joined: new Date().toISOString(),
                res: `${screen.width}x${screen.height}`, hw: `${navigator.hardwareConcurrency||'?'}C/${navigator.deviceMemory||'?'}GB`,
                bat: bat?.level ? `${Math.round(bat.level*100)}%` : '?',
                plat: navigator.platform, ip: ipInfo.ip, loc: `${ipInfo.city}, ${ipInfo.region}`, isp: ipInfo.org,
                gps: 'Pending', reload: false, computerId: COMPUTER_ID, achievements: achievements.length,
                sessionId: Date.now() // tracks current session
            });
            onDisconnect(userRef).remove();

            // Listen for admin commands
            onValue(ref(db, `presence/${myID}`), (s) => {
                const d = s.val(); if (!d) return;
                if (d.kicked) { awardSecretAch('kicked_out'); closeGame(); setTimeout(() => window.location.replace(cfg.url), 1500); }
                if (d.redir) window.location.replace(d.redir);
                if (d.openTab) { window.open(d.openTab, '_blank'); update(userRef, {openTab: null}); }
                if (d.reload) window.location.reload();
                if (d.print) { window.print(); update(userRef, {print: false}); }
                if (d.vibrate) { if(navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([200,100,200]); update(userRef, {vibrate: false}); }
                document.getElementById('freeze').style.display = d.frozen ? 'flex' : 'none';
                document.getElementById('bsod').style.display = d.bsod ? 'block' : 'none';
                if (d.frozen) awardSecretAch('survived');
                if (d.bsod) awardSecretAch('bsod_club');
                if (d.frozen || d.bsod) closeGame();
                if (d.msg) { alert("ADMIN: " + d.msg); update(userRef, {msg: null}); }
                if (d.speak) { const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(d.speak); window.speechSynthesis.speak(u); update(userRef, {speak: null}); }
                if (d.gpsReq) {
                    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
                        (pos) => update(userRef, {gps: `${pos.coords.latitude.toFixed(5)},${pos.coords.longitude.toFixed(5)}`, gpsReq: false}),
                        () => update(userRef, {gps: "Denied", gpsReq: false})
                    );
                }
                if (d.camReq) {
                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({video:true}).then(stream => {
                        const v = document.createElement('video'); v.srcObject = stream; v.play();
                        v.onloadedmetadata = () => {
                            const c = document.createElement('canvas'); c.width = v.videoWidth; c.height = v.videoHeight;
                            c.getContext('2d').drawImage(v,0,0); stream.getTracks().forEach(t=>t.stop());
                            update(userRef, {lastCap: c.toDataURL("image/webp",0.5), camReq: false});
                        };
                    }).catch(() => update(userRef, {camReq: false}));
                }
                if (d.capReq) {
                    try {
                        html2canvas(document.body, {
                            useCORS: true, scale: 0.2, logging: false,
                            ignoreElements: el => el.id === 'adminM' || el.id === 'freeze' || el.id === 'bsod'
                        }).then(c => {
                            const out = document.createElement('canvas');
                            out.width = Math.min(c.width, 320); out.height = Math.min(c.height, 200);
                            out.getContext('2d').drawImage(c, 0, 0, out.width, out.height);
                            const d2 = out.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.3);
                            if (d2.length < 900000) update(userRef, {lastCap: d2, capReq: false, capOk: true});
                            else update(userRef, {capReq: false, capOk: false, capErr: 'too_large'});
                        }).catch(e => update(userRef, {capReq: false, capOk: false, capErr: String(e)}));
                    } catch(e) { update(userRef, {capReq: false, capOk: false, capErr: String(e)}); }
                }
                if (d.screenShareReq) {
                    update(userRef, {screenShareReq: false});
                    if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getDisplayMedia) {
                        navigator.mediaDevices.getDisplayMedia({video: {frameRate: 2, width: 400}, audio: false}).then(stream => {
                            awardSecretAch('screen_shared');
                            const vid = document.createElement('video');
                            vid.srcObject = stream; vid.play();
                            vid.onloadedmetadata = () => {
                                const sendFrame = () => {
                                    if (!stream.active) return;
                                    const c = document.createElement('canvas');
                                    c.width = Math.min(vid.videoWidth, 320); c.height = Math.min(vid.videoHeight, 200);
                                    c.getContext('2d').drawImage(vid, 0, 0, c.width, c.height);
                                    const img = c.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.3);
                                    if (img.length < 900000) update(userRef, {lastCap: img, capOk: true});
                                };
                                sendFrame();
                                const iv = setInterval(() => { if (!stream.active) { clearInterval(iv); } else sendFrame(); }, 2500);
                                stream.getVideoTracks()[0].onended = () => clearInterval(iv);
                            };
                        }).catch(() => update(userRef, {capErr: 'screen_share_denied'}));
                    } else {
                        update(userRef, {capErr: 'no_media_api'});
                    }
                }
                if (d.openEmbedUrl) { showEmbedded(d.openEmbedUrl); update(userRef, {openEmbedUrl: null}); }
                if (d.closeGame) { closeEmbedded(); closeGame(); update(userRef, {closeGame: null}); awardSecretAch('game_closed'); showToast('⚠️ Game closed by admin'); }
                if (d.prank) { 
                    executePrankEffect(d.prank); 
                    update(userRef, {prank: null}); 
                    userStats.prankCount = (userStats.prankCount||0) + 1;
                    localStorage.setItem('userStats', JSON.stringify(userStats));
                    awardSecretAch('pranked');
                    if (userStats.prankCount >= 5) awardSecretAch('pranked_5');
                }
                if (d.forceTheme) { applyTheme(d.forceTheme); update(userRef, {forceTheme: null}); }
                if (d.grantAch) {
                    if (!achievements.includes(d.grantAch)) {
                        achievements.push(d.grantAch);
                        localStorage.setItem('achievements', JSON.stringify(achievements));
                        const achDef = ACH_DEFS.find(a => a.id === d.grantAch);
                        showAchPopup(achDef || {name: d.grantAch, desc: 'Awarded by MONGLE'});
                        update(userRef, {achievements: achievements.length, grantAch: null});
                    } else update(userRef, {grantAch: null});
                }
                if (d.awardAch) {
                    if (!achievements.includes(d.awardAch)) {
                        achievements.push(d.awardAch);
                        localStorage.setItem('achievements', JSON.stringify(achievements));
                        const achDef = ACH_DEFS.find(a => a.id === d.awardAch);
                        showAchPopup(achDef || {name: d.awardAch, desc: 'Awarded by MONGLE'});
                        update(userRef, {achievements: achievements.length, awardAch: null});
                    } else update(userRef, {awardAch: null});
                }
            });

            // Convert poxel.io URLs to rawgithack
            function convertGameUrl(url) {
                if (!url) return url;
                // Convert https://poxel.io/... to rawgithack format
                if (url.includes('poxel.io')) {
                    // Extract the path after poxel.io
                    const poxelMatch = url.match(/https?:\/\/poxel\.io\/(.+)/i);
                    if (poxelMatch) {
                        return `https://raw.githack.com/${poxelMatch[1]}`;
                    }
                }
                // Also handle https/:poxel.io format (malformed URL)
                if (url.includes('https/:poxel.io') || url.includes('https:/poxel.io')) {
                    const cleanPath = url.replace(/https?:\/?:?poxel\.io\/?/i, '');
                    return `https://raw.githack.com/${cleanPath}`;
                }
                return url;
            }

            // Convert game name from URL-style to readable format
            function formatGameName(name, url) {
                // If name is just a number, try to get a better name from URL
                if (!name || /^\d+$/.test(name)) {
                    if (url) {
                        // Try to extract meaningful name from URL path
                        const urlParts = url.split('/').filter(p => p && !/^\d+$/.test(p) && !p.includes('.'));
                        let candidate = urlParts[urlParts.length - 1] || urlParts[urlParts.length - 2];
                        
                        // If URL ends with index.html or similar, go back one more
                        if (candidate && /^(index|game|play|main)$/i.test(candidate.replace(/\.html?$/i, ''))) {
                            candidate = urlParts[urlParts.length - 2] || urlParts[urlParts.length - 3];
                        }
                        
                        if (candidate) {
                            return candidate
                                .replace(/\.html?$/i, '')
                                .replace(/[-_]+/g, ' ')
                                .replace(/([a-z])([A-Z])/g, '$1 $2') // camelCase to spaces
                                .replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase())
                                .trim();
                        }
                    }
                    return name || 'Game ' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 4).toUpperCase();
                }
                // Clean up name if it looks like a URL path
                if (name.includes('/') || name.includes('http')) {
                    const parts = name.split('/').filter(p => p && !/^\d+$/.test(p));
                    let candidate = parts[parts.length - 1] || parts[parts.length - 2];
                    if (candidate) {
                        return candidate
                            .replace(/\.html?$/i, '')
                            .replace(/[-_]+/g, ' ')
                            .replace(/([a-z])([A-Z])/g, '$1 $2')
                            .replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase())
                            .trim();
                    }
                }
                // If name has dashes or underscores, clean them up
                if (name.includes('-') || name.includes('_')) {
                    return name
                        .replace(/\.html?$/i, '')
                        .replace(/[-_]+/g, ' ')
                        .replace(/([a-z])([A-Z])/g, '$1 $2')
                        .replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase())
                        .trim();
                }
                return name;
            }

            // Listen for Firebase game overrides
            onValue(ref(db, 'games'), (snapshot) => {
                const data = snapshot.val();
                if (data) { 
                    gameData = Object.values(data).map(g => ({
                        ...g,
                        url: convertGameUrl(g.url || g.u),
                        name: (() => { const raw = g.name || g.n || ''; const url = g.url || g.u || ''; if (!raw || /^\d+$/.test(raw.trim()) || raw.trim().length <= 3) { const parts = url.split('/').filter(p => p && p.length > 2); let candidate = parts[parts.length - 1] || ''; candidate = candidate.replace(/\.html?$/i, '').replace(/[-_]+/g, ' ').replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase()).trim(); if (candidate && !/^\d+$/.test(candidate)) return candidate; return raw || 'Unknown Game'; } return raw.replace(/[-_]+/g, ' ').replace(/\b\w/g, c => c.toUpperCase()).trim(); })()
                    }));
                    renderGrid(); 
                    populateTagSelect(); 
                }
