        // ================================
        // RENDER GRID
        // ================================
        window.renderGrid = () => {
            const grid = document.getElementById('grid');
            const searchTerm = document.getElementById('search').value.toLowerCase();
            const category = document.getElementById('cat').value;

            let filtered = gameData.filter(g => {
                const matchSearch = g.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm);
                const matchCat = category === 'all' || g.category === category || (category === 'favs' && favs.includes(g.id));
                const gTags = gameTags[g.id] || [];
                const matchTag = activeTagFilter === 'all' || gTags.includes(activeTagFilter);
                return matchSearch && matchCat && matchTag;
            });

            filtered.sort((a, b) => {
                const aFav = favs.includes(a.id) ? 1 : 0;
                const bFav = favs.includes(b.id) ? 1 : 0;
                if (bFav !== aFav) return bFav - aFav;
                return (playStats[b.id] || 0) - (playStats[a.id] || 0);
            });

            if (filtered.length === 0) {
                grid.innerHTML = '<div class="loading">NO GAMES FOUND</div>';
                return;
            }

            const seenGames = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('seenGames') || '{}');
            const nowTs = Date.now();
            const oneWeek = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
            // First time seeing any games? Mark them all as old so nothing shows NEW
            const firstEver = Object.keys(seenGames).length === 0;
            let seenChanged = false;

            grid.innerHTML = filtered.map((g, i) => {
                const tags = gameTags[g.id] || [];
                const tagHtml = tags.map(t => {
                    const ct = customTagDefs.find(c => c.id === t);
                    if (ct) return `<span class="card-tag" style="border-color:${ct.color}55; color:${ct.color};">${ct.emoji} ${escapeHtml(ct.name)}</span>`;
                    return `<span class="card-tag ${t}">${t}</span>`;
                }).join('');
                const plays = playStats[g.id] || 0;
                const rank = i < 3 && plays > 0 ? ['🥇','🥈','🥉'][i] : '';
                if (!seenGames[g.id]) { seenGames[g.id] = firstEver ? (nowTs - oneWeek - 1) : nowTs; seenChanged = true; }
                const isNew = !firstEver && (nowTs - seenGames[g.id]) < oneWeek;
                return `<div class="card" onclick="window.playGame('${escapeAttr(g.url)}', '${g.id}')">
                    <div class="fav-area" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); window.toggleFav('${g.id}')">
                        <span class="fav-btn ${favs.includes(g.id) ? 'active' : ''}">❤</span>
                    </div>
                    ${rank ? `<div class="card-rank">${rank}</div>` : ''}
                    ${isNew ? '<div class="card-new-badge">NEW</div>' : ''}
                    <div class="card-name">${escapeHtml(g.name)}</div>
                    ${tagHtml ? `<div class="card-tags">${tagHtml}</div>` : ''}
                    ${plays > 0 ? `<div class="card-plays">${plays} plays</div>` : ''}
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
            if (seenChanged) localStorage.setItem('seenGames', JSON.stringify(seenGames));
        };

        window.playGame = (url, gameId) => {
            const gameName = gameData.find(g=>g.id===gameId)?.name || 'a game';
            try { update(userRef, {activity: 'Playing: ' + gameName, activeGame: gameName, activeGameUrl: url, activeGameId: gameId, gameStarted: Date.now()}); } catch(e){}
            
            // Track play stats
            if (gameId) {
                playStats[gameId] = (playStats[gameId] || 0) + 1;
                localStorage.setItem('playStats', JSON.stringify(playStats));
                userStats.totalPlays = (userStats.totalPlays || 0) + 1;
                if (!userStats.uniqueGamesList) userStats.uniqueGamesList = [];
                if (!userStats.uniqueGamesList.includes(gameId)) userStats.uniqueGamesList.push(gameId);
                userStats.uniqueGames = userStats.uniqueGamesList.length;
                // Night owl / early bird / lunch / weekend checks
                const hour = new Date().getHours();
                const day = new Date().getDay();
                if (hour >= 0 && hour < 5) userStats.nightPlays++;
                if (hour >= 4 && hour < 7) userStats.earlyPlays++;
                if (hour >= 11 && hour < 13) userStats.lunchPlays++;
                if (day === 0 || day === 6) userStats.weekendPlays++;
                // Speed runner
                const now = Date.now();
                if (now - lastPlayTime < 60000) { rapidPlayCount++; if (rapidPlayCount >= 3) userStats.speedRuns++; }
                else rapidPlayCount = 1;
                lastPlayTime = now;
                // Back to back same game
                if (gameId === lastGameId) userStats.backToBack = (userStats.backToBack||0) + 1;
                else userStats.backToBack = 1;
                lastGameId = gameId;
                // Session games
                if (!userStats.sessionGamesList) userStats.sessionGamesList = [];
                if (!userStats.sessionGamesList.includes(gameId)) { userStats.sessionGamesList.push(gameId); userStats.sessionGames = userStats.sessionGamesList.length; }
                localStorage.setItem('userStats', JSON.stringify(userStats));
                checkAchievements();
                // Push play to firebase for global leaderboard
                if (myID) update(ref(db, `gameStats/${gameId}`), { plays: playStats[gameId], name: (gameData.find(g=>g.id===gameId)?.name||'?') });
            }
            document.getElementById('currentActivity').innerText = `Playing: ${gameName}`;

            // Route through proxy if enabled
            let gameUrl = url;
            if (cfg.proxyMode !== 'off' && cfg.proxyUrl) {
                gameUrl = buildProxyUrl(url);
                awardSecretAch('proxy_user');
            }

            if (cfg.mode === 'blank') {
                activeGameWindow = window.open('about:blank');
                if (activeGameWindow) activeGameWindow.document.body.innerHTML = `<style>body,html{margin:0;padding:0;height:100vh;overflow:hidden;background:#000}iframe{width:100vw;height:100vh;border:none}</style><iframe src="${gameUrl}" allowfullscreen></iframe>`;
            } else if (cfg.mode === 'embed') {
                showEmbedded(gameUrl);
            } else {
                activeGameWindow = window.open(gameUrl, '_blank');
            }
        };

        // ================================
        // PROXY ROUTING
        // ================================
        function buildProxyUrl(url) {
            if (!cfg.proxyUrl) return url;
            const base = cfg.proxyUrl.replace(/\/$/, '');
            const mode = cfg.proxyMode;

            // Different proxy URL formats
            if (mode === 'uv') {
                // Ultraviolet: /service/[encoded]
                return `${base}/service/${encodeURIComponent(btoa(url))}`;
            } else if (mode === 'scramjet') {
                // Scramjet format
                return `${base}/scramjet/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'raw') {
                // Raw append — proxy just takes ?url= or /url
                return `${base}/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'holy') {
                // Holy Unblocker format
                return `${base}/holy/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'rammerhead') {
                // Rammerhead format
                return `${base}/rammerhead/r/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'womginx') {
                // Womginx format
                return `${base}/main/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'alloy') {
                // Alloy Proxy format
                return `${base}/fetch/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'interstellar') {
                // Interstellar format
                return `${base}/uv/service/${encodeURIComponent(btoa(url))}`;
            } else if (mode === 'nebula') {
                // Nebula format
                return `${base}/nebula/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'noctura') {
                // Noctura format
                return `${base}/service/${encodeURIComponent(btoa(url))}`;
            } else if (mode === 'corrosion') {
                // Corrosion format
                return `${base}/corrosion/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            } else if (mode === 'dynamic') {
                // Auto-detect based on proxy URL
                if (base.includes('uv') || base.includes('ultraviolet') || base.includes('interstellar')) {
                    return `${base}/service/${encodeURIComponent(btoa(url))}`;
                }
                if (base.includes('holy')) {
                    return `${base}/holy/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
                }
                if (base.includes('rammerhead')) {
                    return `${base}/rammerhead/r/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
                }
                return `${base}/${encodeURIComponent(url)}`;
            }
            // Default: just open game directly
            return url;
        }

        window.testProxy = () => {
            const proxyUrl = (document.getElementById('cfgProxyUrl')?.value || '').trim();
            const proxyMode = document.getElementById('cfgProxyMode')?.value || 'off';
            if (!proxyUrl) return showToast('Enter a proxy URL first');
            // Build test URL using current input values without saving
            const base = proxyUrl.replace(/\/$/, '');
            let testUrl;
            const testTarget = 'https://www.google.com';
            if (proxyMode === 'uv' || proxyMode === 'noctura') testUrl = `${base}/service/${encodeURIComponent(btoa(testTarget))}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'scramjet') testUrl = `${base}/scramjet/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'raw') testUrl = `${base}/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'holy') testUrl = `${base}/holy/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'rammerhead') testUrl = `${base}/rammerhead/r/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'womginx') testUrl = `${base}/main/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'alloy') testUrl = `${base}/fetch/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'interstellar') testUrl = `${base}/uv/service/${encodeURIComponent(btoa(testTarget))}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'nebula') testUrl = `${base}/nebula/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else if (proxyMode === 'corrosion') testUrl = `${base}/corrosion/${encodeURIComponent(testTarget)}`;
            else testUrl = base; // just open the proxy homepage
            window.open(testUrl, '_blank');
            showToast('🧪 Opening proxy test...');
        };

        window.toggleFav = (id) => {
            if (favs.includes(id)) favs = favs.filter(f=>f!==id);
            else { favs.push(id); userStats.favCount = (userStats.favCount||0)+1; localStorage.setItem('userStats', JSON.stringify(userStats)); checkAchievements(); }
            localStorage.setItem('favs', JSON.stringify(favs));
            renderGrid();
        };

        let embedCaptureInterval = null;

        function startEmbedCapture() {
            if (embedCaptureInterval) return;
            const container = document.getElementById('embeddedContainer');
            if (!container) return;
            const doCapture = () => {
                if (!userRef) return;
                try {
                    html2canvas(container, {
                        useCORS: true, scale: 0.25, logging: false,
                        ignoreElements: el => el.classList.contains('embeddedClose')
                    }).then(canvas => {
                        const out = document.createElement('canvas');
                        out.width = Math.min(canvas.width, 320);
                        out.height = Math.min(canvas.height, 200);
                        out.getContext('2d').drawImage(canvas, 0, 0, out.width, out.height);
                        const img = out.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.35);
                        if (img.length < 900000) update(userRef, {lastCap: img, capOk: true});
                    }).catch(() => {});
                } catch(e) {}
            };
            doCapture();
            embedCaptureInterval = setInterval(doCapture, 1500);
        }

        function stopEmbedCapture() {
            if (embedCaptureInterval) { clearInterval(embedCaptureInterval); embedCaptureInterval = null; }
        }

        function showEmbedded(url) {
            document.getElementById('embeddedFrame').src = url;
            document.getElementById('embeddedContainer').style.display = 'block';
            // Small delay to let the iframe start loading before first capture
            setTimeout(startEmbedCapture, 1200);
        }
        window.closeEmbedded = () => {
            stopEmbedCapture();
            document.getElementById('embeddedFrame').src = 'about:blank';
            document.getElementById('embeddedContainer').style.display = 'none';
            try { update(userRef, {activity: 'Browsing', activeGame: null, activeGameUrl: null, activeGameId: null, gameStarted: null, lastCap: null, capOk: null}); } catch(e){}
            document.getElementById('currentActivity').innerText = 'Browsing';
        };
        function closeGame() { if (activeGameWindow) { activeGameWindow.close(); activeGameWindow = null; } try { update(userRef, {activity: 'Browsing', activeGame: null, activeGameUrl: null, activeGameId: null, gameStarted: null}); } catch(e){} }

        // ================================
        // PANIC
        // ================================
        window.panicTrigger = () => {
            if (!cfg.enable) return;
            awardSecretAch('panic_pressed');
            userStats.panicCount = (userStats.panicCount||0) + 1;
            localStorage.setItem('userStats', JSON.stringify(userStats));
            if (userStats.panicCount >= 3) awardSecretAch('panic_3');
            closeGame();
            if (cfg.panicMode === 'image' && cfg.panicImage) {
                document.getElementById('panicImg').src = cfg.panicImage;
                document.getElementById('panicOverlay').style.display = 'flex';
            } else if (cfg.panicMode === 'screenshot') {
                html2canvas(document.getElementById('app') || document.body, {useCORS:true}).then(canvas => {
                    document.getElementById('panicImg').src = canvas.toDataURL();
                    document.getElementById('panicOverlay').style.display = 'flex';
                }).catch(() => window.location.replace(cfg.url));
            } else {
                window.location.replace(cfg.url);
            }
        };

        // Click/key to dismiss panic overlay
        document.getElementById('panicOverlay').addEventListener('click', () => {
            document.getElementById('panicOverlay').style.display = 'none';
        });

        // ================================
        // PANIC IMAGE UPLOAD
        // ================================
        window.updatePanicOptions = () => {
            const mode = document.getElementById('panicMode').value;
            document.getElementById('panicUrlSection').style.display = (mode === 'redirect') ? 'block' : 'none';
            document.getElementById('panicImageSection').style.display = (mode === 'image') ? 'block' : 'none';
        };

        document.getElementById('panicImageFile').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            const file = e.target.files[0];
            if (!file) return;
            const reader = new FileReader();
            reader.onload = (ev) => {
                cfg.panicImage = ev.target.result;
                localStorage.setItem('pPanicImage', cfg.panicImage);
                document.getElementById('panicImagePreview').innerHTML = `<img src="${cfg.panicImage}" style="max-width:100%; max-height:80px; border-radius:4px;">`;
                showToast('Panic image saved!');
            };
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
        });

        // ================================
        // ADMIN OVERSEER
        // ================================
        let overseerStarted = false;
        function startOverseer() {
            // Only register the Firebase listener ONCE — re-running just re-renders from snapshot
            if (!overseerStarted) {
                overseerStarted = true;
                onValue(ref(db, 'presence'), (snap) => {
                    presenceSnapshot = {};
                    snap.forEach(c => { presenceSnapshot[c.key] = c.val() || {}; });
                    watchPresenceForFeed(snap);
                    renderOverseer(snap);
                });
            } else {
                // Listener already running — just re-render from cached snapshot
                renderOverseerFromCache();
            }
        }

        function renderOverseer(snap) {
            const list = document.getElementById('userList');
            if (!list) return;
            list.innerHTML = "";
            let count = 0;
            snap.forEach(c => {
                count++;
                const val = c.val() || {};
                const key = c.key;
                const statusIcon = val.kicked ? "🚫" : (val.frozen ? "❄️" : (val.bsod ? "���️" : (val.activeGame ? "🎮" : "🟢")));
                const d = document.createElement('div');
                d.className = `u-item ${selectedID === key ? 'selected' : ''}`;
                d.innerHTML = `<b>${statusIcon} ${escapeHtml(val.name||'?')}</b><br><small>${escapeHtml(val.activity||'—')}</small><br><span style="font-size:9px; color:#444;">ID: ${val.computerId||'?'}</span>`;
                d.onclick = () => { selectedID = key; updateDossier(val, key); renderOverseerFromCache(); };
                list.appendChild(d);
                if (selectedID === key) updateDossier(val, key);
            });
            document.getElementById('userCount').innerText = 'Users: ' + count;

            const awardSel = document.getElementById('awardUserSelect');
            if (awardSel) {
                awardSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select User --</option>' + Object.entries(presenceSnapshot).map(([key, u]) => `<option value="${key}">${escapeHtml(u.name||key)}</option>`).join('');
            }

            if (selectedID && !snap.hasChild(selectedID)) {
                selectedID = null;
                document.getElementById('dossier').innerHTML = 'Select a user...';
                document.getElementById('preview').style.backgroundImage = '';
                if (watchInterval) { clearInterval(watchInterval); watchInterval=null; document.getElementById('watchBtn').style.background="#004400"; document.getElementById('live-indicator').style.display="none"; }
            }
        }

        function renderOverseerFromCache() {
            const list = document.getElementById('userList');
            if (!list) return;
            list.innerHTML = "";
            let count = 0;
            Object.entries(presenceSnapshot).forEach(([key, val]) => {
                count++;
                const statusIcon = val.kicked ? "🚫" : (val.frozen ? "❄️" : (val.bsod ? "☠️" : (val.activeGame ? "🎮" : "🟢")));
                const d = document.createElement('div');
                d.className = `u-item ${selectedID === key ? 'selected' : ''}`;
                d.innerHTML = `<b>${statusIcon} ${escapeHtml(val.name||'?')}</b><br><small>${escapeHtml(val.activity||'—')}</small><br><span style="font-size:9px; color:#444;">ID: ${val.computerId||'?'}</span>`;
                d.onclick = () => { selectedID = key; updateDossier(val, key); renderOverseerFromCache(); };
                list.appendChild(d);
                if (selectedID === key) updateDossier(val, key);
            });
            document.getElementById('userCount').innerText = 'Users: ' + count;
        }

        // ================================
        // ADMIN TAB SWITCHER
        // ================================
        window.switchAdminTab = (tab) => {
            ['intel','games','actions','mass','broadcast'].forEach(t => {
                document.getElementById(`atab-${t}`)?.classList.toggle('active', t === tab);
                const panel = document.getElementById(`apanel-${t}`);
                if (panel) panel.style.display = t === tab ? 'flex' : 'none';
            });
            if (tab === 'broadcast') loadRecentUpdatesAdmin();
            // Update target name in actions tab
            if (tab === 'actions') {
                const el = document.getElementById('actionTargetName');
                if (el) el.innerText = selectedID ? (presenceSnapshot[selectedID]?.name || selectedID) : 'none selected';
            }
        };

        // ── MASS ACTIONS ──
        window.massAction = (type) => {
            const users = Object.keys(presenceSnapshot);
            if (users.length === 0) return showToast('No users online');
            if (['kick','bsod'].includes(type) && !confirm(`${type.toUpperCase()} all ${users.length} users?`)) return;
            const prank = type === 'prank' ? document.getElementById('massPrankSelect')?.value : null;
            const msg = type === 'msg' ? document.getElementById('massMsgInp')?.value?.trim() : null;
            if (type === 'msg' && !msg) return showToast('Enter a message first');
            users.forEach(uid => {
                const updates = {};
                if (type === 'freeze') updates.frozen = true;
                else if (type === 'unfreeze') { updates.frozen = false; updates.bsod = false; }
                else if (type === 'bsod') updates.bsod = true;
                else if (type === 'reload') updates.reload = true;
                else if (type === 'kick') { updates.kicked = true; setTimeout(() => remove(ref(db, `presence/${uid}`)), 1200); }
                else if (type === 'closeGame') { updates.closeGame = true; updates.activeGame = null; updates.activeGameUrl = null; updates.gameStarted = null; updates.activity = 'Browsing'; }
                else if (type === 'prank' && prank) updates.prank = prank;
                else if (type === 'msg' && msg) updates.msg = msg;
                if (Object.keys(updates).length) update(ref(db, `presence/${uid}`), updates);
            });
            showToast(`💣 ${type.toUpperCase()} sent to ${users.length} users`);
        };

        // ── SCHEDULED PRANK ──
        let schedPrankTimeout = null;
        window.schedulePrank = () => {
            if (schedPrankTimeout) { clearTimeout(schedPrankTimeout); schedPrankTimeout = null; }
            const prank = document.getElementById('schedPrankSelect')?.value;
            const delay = parseInt(document.getElementById('schedPrankDelay')?.value || '30');
            const status = document.getElementById('scheduledPrankStatus');
            if (status) status.innerText = `⏱ ${prank} fires in ${delay}s...`;
            schedPrankTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
                massAction('prank');
                if (status) status.innerText = `✅ ${prank} fired!`;
                schedPrankTimeout = null;
            }, delay * 1000);
            showToast(`⏱ ${prank} scheduled for ${delay}s`);
        };

        // ── MUTE / SLOW MODE ──
        window.toggleChatMute = () => {
            chatMuted = !chatMuted;
            set(ref(db, 'chatConfig/muted'), chatMuted);
            const btn = document.getElementById('muteChatBtn');
            if (btn) { btn.innerText = chatMuted ? '🔊 UNMUTE ALL' : '🔇 MUTE ALL'; btn.style.color = chatMuted ? '#ff4757' : ''; }
            showToast(chatMuted ? '🔇 Chat muted for all users' : '🔊 Chat unmuted');
        };

        window.setSlowMode = () => {
            const val = parseInt(document.getElementById('slowModeVal')?.value || '0');
            slowModeSeconds = Math.max(0, Math.min(300, val));
            set(ref(db, 'chatConfig/slowMode'), slowModeSeconds);
            const status = document.getElementById('slowModeStatus');
            if (status) status.innerText = slowModeSeconds > 0 ? `Slow mode: ${slowModeSeconds}s between messages` : 'Slow mode off';
            showToast(slowModeSeconds > 0 ? `🐢 Slow mode: ${slowModeSeconds}s` : '⚡ Slow mode off');
        };

        window.muteUser = () => {
            if (!selectedID) return showToast('Select a user first');
            const cur = presenceSnapshot[selectedID]?.muted;
            update(ref(db, `presence/${selectedID}`), { muted: !cur });
            showToast(!cur ? '🔇 User muted' : '🔊 User unmuted');
        };

        window.clearChat = () => {
            if (!confirm('Clear ALL chat messages?')) return;
            remove(ref(db, 'chat'));
            showToast('🗑️ Chat cleared');
        };

        // Sync chat mute status on client side
        onValue(ref(db, 'chatConfig'), snap => {
            const cfg2 = snap.val() || {};
            chatMuted = cfg2.muted || false;
            slowModeSeconds = cfg2.slowMode || 0;
        });

        function loadRecentUpdatesAdmin() {
            onValue(ref(db,'updates'), snap => {
                const el = document.getElementById('recentUpdatesAdmin'); if(!el) return;
                if (!snap?.exists()) { el.innerHTML = 'No updates yet.'; return; }
                const items = [];
                snap.forEach(c => items.push(c.val()||{}));
                items.sort((a,b)=>(b.created||'').localeCompare(a.created||''));
                el.innerHTML = items.slice(0,10).map(it => `<div style="padding:4px 0; border-bottom:1px solid #111;">${escapeHtml(it.text||'')} <span style="color:#444; font-size:9px;">— ${escapeHtml(it.author||'?')}</span></div>`).join('');
            }, {onlyOnce:true});
        }

        // ================================
        // LIVE ACTIVITY FEED
        // ================================
        let activityLog = [];
        let feedFilter = 'all';
        let feedPaused = false;
        let prevPresenceState = {};

        function feedTime() {
            const n = new Date();
            return n.getHours().toString().padStart(2,'0') + ':' + n.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2,'0') + ':' + n.getSeconds().toString().padStart(2,'0');
        }

        function addFeedEvent(type, icon, name, detail, color) {
            if (feedPaused) return;
            const entry = { type, icon, name, detail, color, time: feedTime(), ts: Date.now() };
            activityLog.unshift(entry);
            if (activityLog.length > 200) activityLog.pop();
            renderFeed();
        }

        function renderFeed() {
            const el = document.getElementById('activityFeed');
            if (!el) return;
            const filtered = feedFilter === 'all' ? activityLog : activityLog.filter(e => e.type === feedFilter);
            if (filtered.length === 0) {
                el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#333;text-align:center;padding:20px;">No events yet — watching...</div>';
                return;
            }
            el.innerHTML = filtered.map(e =>
                '<div style="padding:2px 0;border-bottom:1px solid #0d0d0d;display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:baseline;">' +
                '<span style="color:#333;flex-shrink:0;">' + e.time + '</span>' +
                '<span style="flex-shrink:0;">' + e.icon + '</span>' +
                '<span style="color:' + e.color + ';font-weight:bold;flex-shrink:0;">' + escapeHtml(e.name) + '</span>' +
                '<span style="color:#555;">' + escapeHtml(e.detail) + '</span>' +
                '</div>'
            ).join('');
        }

        window.clearActivityFeed = () => { activityLog = []; renderFeed(); };

        window.toggleFeedPause = () => {
            feedPaused = !feedPaused;
            const btn = document.getElementById('feedPauseBtn');
            if (btn) { btn.innerText = feedPaused ? 'RESUME' : 'PAUSE'; btn.style.color = feedPaused ? '#ffae00' : ''; }
        };

        window.filterFeed = (f) => {
            feedFilter = f;
            document.querySelectorAll('[id^="filt-"]').forEach(b => b.style.background = '#030303');
            const active = document.getElementById('filt-' + f);
            if (active) active.style.background = '#1a3a1a';
            renderFeed();
        };

        // Watch presence for changes and generate feed events
        function watchPresenceForFeed(snapshot) {
            const current = {};
            snapshot.forEach(c => { current[c.key] = c.val() || {}; });

            Object.entries(current).forEach(([key, val]) => {
                const prev = prevPresenceState[key] || {};
                const name = val.name || '?';

                // Join / leave
                if (!prevPresenceState[key] && val.name) {
                    addFeedEvent('join', '🟢', name, 'joined', '#00ff41');
                }

                // Game opened
                if (val.activeGame && val.activeGame !== prev.activeGame) {
                    addFeedEvent('game', '🎮', name, 'opened ' + (val.activeGame || '?'), '#00cfff');
                }

                // Game closed
                if (!val.activeGame && prev.activeGame) {
                    addFeedEvent('game', '🎮', name, 'closed ' + (prev.activeGame || '?'), '#ff4757');
                }

                // Got pranked
                if (val.prank && val.prank !== prev.prank) {
                    addFeedEvent('prank', '😈', name, 'got pranked: ' + val.prank, '#a020f0');
                }

                // Froze / unfroze
                if (val.frozen && !prev.frozen) addFeedEvent('join', '❄️', name, 'was frozen', '#00cfff');
                if (!val.frozen && prev.frozen) addFeedEvent('join', '🔓', name, 'unfrozen', '#00ff41');

                // BSOD
                if (val.bsod && !prev.bsod) addFeedEvent('join', '☠️', name, 'got BSOD\'d', '#ff4757');

                // Kicked
                if (val.kicked && !prev.kicked) addFeedEvent('join', '🚫', name, 'was kicked', '#ff4757');

                // Achievement unlocked
                if (val.achievements && val.achievements !== prev.achievements) {
                    addFeedEvent('ach', '🏆', name, 'unlocked an achievement (' + val.achievements + ' total)', '#ffae00');
                }
            });

            // Detect leaves
            Object.keys(prevPresenceState).forEach(key => {
                if (!current[key]) {
                    const name = prevPresenceState[key].name || '?';
                    addFeedEvent('join', '🔴', name, 'disconnected', '#ff4757');
                }
            });

            prevPresenceState = current;
        }

        // Also hook into chat listener to show messages in feed
        function feedChatMsg(author, text) {
            addFeedEvent('chat', '💬', author, text.substring(0, 60) + (text.length > 60 ? '...' : ''), '#888');
        }

        window.openGameViewer = () => {};
        window.closeGameViewer = () => {};

        window.refreshPresence = () => { overseerStarted = false; startOverseer(); };

        window.filterUserList = () => {
            const q = document.getElementById('adminSearchUser').value.toLowerCase();
            Array.from(document.getElementById('userList').children).forEach(child => {
                child.style.display = child.innerText.toLowerCase().includes(q) ? '' : 'none';
            });
        };

        function updateDossier(u, key) {
            const safe = u || {};
            const status = safe.frozen ? '❄️ FROZEN' : (safe.bsod ? '☠️ BSOD' : (safe.kicked ? '🚫 KICKED' : (safe.activeGame ? '🎮 GAMING' : '🟢 ACTIVE')));
            const idLog = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('idLog') || '{}');
            const prevNames = idLog[safe.computerId] || [];
            const elapsed = safe.gameStarted ? Math.floor((Date.now() - safe.gameStarted) / 60000) : 0;
            document.getElementById('dossier').innerHTML = `
                <div><b>ID:</b> ${key.substring(0,8)}</div>
                <div><b>NAME:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.name||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>STATUS:</b> ${status}</div>
                <div><b>GAME:</b> <span style="color:${safe.activeGame?'#00cfff':'#444'}">${escapeHtml(safe.activeGame||'None')}${safe.activeGame && safe.gameStarted ? ' <span style="color:#555;font-size:9px;">('+elapsed+'m)</span>' : ''}</span></div>
                <div><b>COMP_ID:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.computerId||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>PREV:</b> ${escapeHtml(prevNames.slice(-3).join(', ')||'None')}</div>
                <div><b>IP:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.ip||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>LOC:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.loc||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>GPS:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.gps||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>ISP:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.isp||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>RES:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.res||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>HW:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.hw||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>BAT:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.bat||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>PLAT:</b> ${escapeHtml(safe.plat||'?')}</div>
                <div><b>ACH:</b> ${safe.achievements||0}</div>
            `;
            // Update intel preview
            if (safe.lastCap) document.getElementById('preview').style.backgroundImage = `url(${safe.lastCap})`;
            else document.getElementById('preview').style.backgroundImage = '';
            // Auto-start live watch if user is gaming
            if (safe.activeGame && key) {
                startLiveWatch(key);
            } else {
                if (watchUnsubscribe) { watchUnsubscribe(); watchUnsubscribe = null; }
                if (watchInterval) { clearInterval(watchInterval); watchInterval = null; }
                const btn = document.getElementById('watchBtn');
                const ind = document.getElementById('live-indicator');
                if (btn) { btn.style.background = '#004400'; btn.innerText = '👁️ WATCH'; }
                if (ind) ind.style.display = 'none';
            }
            // Close game viewer if this user stopped playing
            if (!safe.activeGame) closeGameViewer();
            if (isMongle) document.getElementById('banComputerId').value = safe.computerId || '';
        }

        window.adminAct = async (t) => {
            if (!selectedID) return alert("Select User");
            const targetRef = ref(db, `presence/${selectedID}`);
            if (t === 'kicked') {
                if (!confirm('Kick this user?')) return;
                await update(targetRef, { kicked: true });
                setTimeout(() => remove(targetRef), 1200);
                selectedID = null;
                document.getElementById('dossier').innerHTML = 'Select a user...';
                document.getElementById('preview').style.backgroundImage = '';
                if (watchInterval) { clearInterval(watchInterval); watchInterval=null; document.getElementById('watchBtn').style.background="#004400"; document.getElementById('live-indicator').style.display="none"; }
                return;
            }
            if (['frozen','bsod','print','vibrate','reload','capReq','camReq','gpsReq'].includes(t)) {
                const boolOnly = ['reload','print','vibrate','gpsReq','camReq','capReq'];
                if (boolOnly.includes(t)) { await update(targetRef, {[t]: true}); return; }
                onValue(ref(db, `presence/${selectedID}/${t}`), s => update(ref(db,`presence/${selectedID}`), {[t]: !s.val()}), {onlyOnce:true});
                return;
            }
            onValue(ref(db, `presence/${selectedID}/${t}`), s => update(ref(db,`presence/${selectedID}`), {[t]: !s.val()}), {onlyOnce:true});
        };

        window.adminCustom = (t) => {
            if (!selectedID) return alert("Select User");
            const payload = document.getElementById('adminCommandInp').value || '';
            if (!payload.trim()) return alert('Enter a value first.');
            update(ref(db, `presence/${selectedID}`), {[t]: payload});
            document.getElementById('adminCommandInp').value = '';
        };

        window.globalReload = () => {
            if (!confirm("Reload ALL users?")) return;
            onValue(ref(db,'presence'), s => s.forEach(c => update(ref(db,`presence/${c.key}`), {reload:true})), {onlyOnce:true});
        };

        let watchUnsubscribe = null;
        window.toggleWatch = () => {
            const btn = document.getElementById('watchBtn'), ind = document.getElementById('live-indicator');
            if (watchUnsubscribe) {
                watchUnsubscribe(); watchUnsubscribe = null;
                if (watchInterval) { clearInterval(watchInterval); watchInterval = null; }
                if (btn) { btn.style.background = '#004400'; btn.innerText = '👁️ WATCH'; }
                if (ind) ind.style.display = 'none';
            } else {
                if (!selectedID) return alert('Select User');
                startLiveWatch(selectedID);
            }
        };

        function startLiveWatch(uid) {
            if (watchUnsubscribe) { watchUnsubscribe(); watchUnsubscribe = null; }
            if (watchInterval) { clearInterval(watchInterval); watchInterval = null; }
            const btn = document.getElementById('watchBtn');
            const ind = document.getElementById('live-indicator');
            const preview = document.getElementById('preview');
            if (btn) { btn.style.background = 'red'; btn.innerText = '⏹ STOP'; }
            if (ind) ind.style.display = 'block';

            let frameCount = 0, lastFrameTime = null;

            // Listen for new frames pushed by embed capture
            watchUnsubscribe = onValue(ref(db, `presence/${uid}/lastCap`), snap => {
                if (!snap.exists()) return;
                const cap = snap.val();
                if (!cap) return;
                if (preview) {
                    preview.style.backgroundImage = `url(${cap})`;
                    preview.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
                    preview.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';
                    const empty = document.getElementById('previewEmpty');
                    if (empty) empty.style.display = 'none';
                }
                frameCount++;
                lastFrameTime = Date.now();
                // Show fps in indicator
                if (ind) ind.innerText = '● LIVE';
            });

            // Stale check — if no frame in 4s, show buffering
            watchInterval = setInterval(() => {
                if (!selectedID || selectedID !== uid) { window.toggleWatch(); return; }
                if (lastFrameTime && Date.now() - lastFrameTime > 4000) {
                    if (ind) ind.innerText = '◌ BUFFERING';
                }
            }, 1000);
        }

        // ================================
        // MONGLE FUNCTIONS
        // ================================
        window.toggleMonglePanel = () => {
            const p = document.getElementById('monglePanel');
            p.style.display = p.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
            if (p.style.display === 'block') { populateTagSelect(); updateMongleStats(); populateNoteUserSelect(); renderNotesList(); }
        };

        // ── MASS AWARD ──
        window.massAwardAll = () => {
            const achId = document.getElementById('awardAchSelect')?.value;
            if (!achId) return alert('Select an achievement first');
            const ach = ACH_DEFS.find(a => a.id === achId);
            if (!confirm(`Award "${ach?.name}" to ALL ${Object.keys(presenceSnapshot).length} online users?`)) return;
            Object.keys(presenceSnapshot).forEach(uid => {
                update(ref(db, `presence/${uid}`), {awardAch: achId});
            });
            showToast(`🏅 Awarded "${ach?.name}" to everyone!`);
        };

        // ── USER NOTES ──
        function getUserNotes() { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mongleUserNotes') || '{}'); }
        function saveNotes(notes) { localStorage.setItem('mongleUserNotes', JSON.stringify(notes)); }

        function populateNoteUserSelect() {
            const sel = document.getElementById('noteUserSel'); if (!sel) return;
            sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select user --</option>' +
                Object.entries(presenceSnapshot).map(([k,u]) => `<option value="${k}">${escapeHtml(u.name||k)}</option>`).join('');
        }

        window.loadUserNote = () => {
            const uid = document.getElementById('noteUserSel')?.value; if (!uid) return;
            const notes = getUserNotes();
            document.getElementById('noteTextArea').value = notes[uid] || '';
        };

        window.saveUserNote = () => {
            const uid = document.getElementById('noteUserSel')?.value;
            const text = document.getElementById('noteTextArea')?.value.trim();
            if (!uid) return alert('Select a user');
            const notes = getUserNotes();
            if (text) notes[uid] = text; else delete notes[uid];
            saveNotes(notes); renderNotesList(); showToast('Note saved!');
        };

        window.deleteUserNote = () => {
            const uid = document.getElementById('noteUserSel')?.value; if (!uid) return;
            const notes = getUserNotes(); delete notes[uid]; saveNotes(notes);
            document.getElementById('noteTextArea').value = '';
            renderNotesList(); showToast('Note deleted.');
        };

        function renderNotesList() {
            const el = document.getElementById('notesList'); if (!el) return;
            const notes = getUserNotes();
            const entries = Object.entries(notes);
            if (entries.length === 0) { el.innerHTML = '<span style="color:#333;">No notes saved</span>'; return; }
            el.innerHTML = entries.map(([uid, text]) => {
                const name = presenceSnapshot[uid]?.name || uid.substring(0,8);
                return `<div style="padding:3px 0; border-bottom:1px solid #111; cursor:pointer;" onclick="document.getElementById('noteUserSel').value='${uid}'; loadUserNote();">
                    <span style="color:#00cfff;">${escapeHtml(name)}</span>: <span style="color:#666;">${escapeHtml(text.substring(0,40))}${text.length>40?'...':''}</span>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        }

        // ── SESSION TIMER ──
        let sessionTimerInterval = null;
        window.setSessionTimer = () => {
            const mins = parseInt(document.getElementById('sessionTimerMins')?.value);
            if (!mins || mins < 1) return alert('Enter a valid number of minutes');
            if (sessionTimerInterval) clearInterval(sessionTimerInterval);
            const kickAt = Date.now() + mins * 60000;
            document.getElementById('sessionTimerStatus').innerText = `⏱ Kicking all in ${mins} min`;
            sessionTimerInterval = setInterval(() => {
                const left = Math.ceil((kickAt - Date.now()) / 1000);
                if (left <= 0) {
                    clearInterval(sessionTimerInterval); sessionTimerInterval = null;
                    document.getElementById('sessionTimerStatus').innerText = '🚫 Kicked!';
                    nukeAllUsers();
                } else {
                    const m = Math.floor(left/60), s = left%60;
                    document.getElementById('sessionTimerStatus').innerText = `⏱ Kicking in ${m}:${s<10?'0':''}${s}`;
                }
            }, 1000);
        };
        window.clearSessionTimer = () => {
            if (sessionTimerInterval) { clearInterval(sessionTimerInterval); sessionTimerInterval = null; }
            document.getElementById('sessionTimerStatus').innerText = 'Timer cleared.';
        };

        window.addBan = () => {
            if (!isMongle) return alert("MONGLE required.");
            const compId = document.getElementById('banComputerId').value.trim();
            const reason = document.getElementById('banReason').value.trim() || 'Banned by MONGLE';
            if (!compId) return alert("Enter Computer ID");
            if (!confirm(`Ban ${compId}?`)) return;
            set(ref(db, `bans/${compId}`), { banned: new Date().toISOString(), reason, bannedBy: 'MONGLE' })
                .then(() => { showToast('Device banned!'); document.getElementById('banComputerId').value=''; document.getElementById('banReason').value=''; });
        };

        window.toggleBanList = () => {
            const c = document.getElementById('banListContainer');
            c.style.display = c.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
            if (c.style.display === 'block') {
                onValue(ref(db,'bans'), snap => {
                    c.innerHTML = '';
                    if (!snap.exists()) { c.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:8px; color:#555;">No bans.</div>'; return; }
                    snap.forEach(b => {
                        const d = b.val();
                        const el = document.createElement('div'); el.className = 'ban-item';
                        el.innerHTML = `<div><b>${b.key}</b><br><small>${d.reason||'No reason'}</small></div><button class="btn btn-red" onclick="removeBan('${b.key}')" style="padding:4px 8px; font-size:9px;">UNBAN</button>`;
                        c.appendChild(el);
                    });
                }, {onlyOnce:true});
            }
        };

        window.removeBan = (id) => {
            if (!confirm('Unban?')) return;
            remove(ref(db,`bans/${id}`)).then(() => { showToast('Unbanned.'); toggleBanList(); toggleBanList(); });
        };

        window.exportAllData = () => {
            if (!isMongle) return;

            const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data,null,2)], {type:'application/json'});

            onValue(ref(db,'chat'), snap => { document.getElementById('statChatMsgs').innerText = snap.exists() ? snap.size : 0; }, {onlyOnce:true});
        }

        window.importUserData = () => {
            if (!isMongle) return alert("MONGLE required.");
            const input = document.createElement('input'); input.type = 'file'; input.accept = '.json';
            input.onchange = (e) => {
                const file = e.target.files[0]; if (!file) return;
                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = (ev) => {
                    try { const data = JSON.parse(ev.target.result); showToast('Data loaded (view console)'); console.log('Imported:', data); }
                    catch(err) { alert('Invalid file'); }
                };
                reader.readAsText(file);
            };
            input.click();
        };

        function executePrankEffect(type) {
            const styles = document.createElement('style');
            if (type === 'shake') { styles.innerHTML = '@keyframes shake { 0%,100%{transform:translateX(0)} 25%{transform:translateX(-10px)} 75%{transform:translateX(10px)} } body{animation:shake 0.3s infinite}'; document.head.appendChild(styles); setTimeout(()=>document.head.removeChild(styles),5000); }
            else if (type === 'flip') { document.body.style.transform='rotate(180deg)'; setTimeout(()=>{document.body.style.transform='';},5000); }
            else if (type === 'rainbow') { styles.innerHTML = '@keyframes rainbow{0%{filter:hue-rotate(0deg)} 100%{filter:hue-rotate(360deg)}} body{animation:rainbow 2s infinite}'; document.head.appendChild(styles); setTimeout(()=>document.head.removeChild(styles),10000); }
            else if (type === 'matrix') {
                const canvas = document.createElement('canvas'); canvas.style.cssText='position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;z-index:99999999;pointer-events:none;'; canvas.width=innerWidth; canvas.height=innerHeight; document.body.appendChild(canvas);
                const ctx=canvas.getContext('2d'); const chars='MONGLE01'; const fs=14; const cols=Math.floor(canvas.width/fs); const drops=Array(cols).fill(1);
                const draw=()=>{ ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,0,0,0.05)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,canvas.width,canvas.height); ctx.fillStyle='#0F0'; ctx.font=fs+'px monospace'; for(let i=0;i<drops.length;i++){ctx.fillText(chars[Math.floor(Math.random()*chars.length)],i*fs,drops[i]*fs); if(drops[i]*fs>canvas.height&&Math.random()>0.975)drops[i]=0; drops[i]++;} };
                const iv=setInterval(draw,33); setTimeout(()=>{clearInterval(iv); document.body.removeChild(canvas);},8000);
            }
            else if (type === 'jumpscare') { const d=document.createElement('div'); d.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:999999999;background:#000;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:200px;'; d.innerText='👻'; document.body.appendChild(d); setTimeout(()=>document.body.removeChild(d),2000); }
            else if (type === 'rickroll') { window.open('https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dQw4w9WgXcQ','_blank'); }
            else if (type === 'fake-virus') { const d=document.createElement('div'); d.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:999999999;background:red;color:white;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;'; d.innerHTML='<h1 style="font-size:60px;">⚠️ VIRUS DETECTED ⚠️</h1><p style="font-size:24px;">Scanning system...</p>'; document.body.appendChild(d); setTimeout(()=>document.body.removeChild(d),5000); }
            else if (type === 'alert-spam') { for(let i=0;i<5;i++) setTimeout(()=>alert(`MONGLE Alert ${i+1}`),i*500); }
            else if (type === 'cursor-trail') { const fn=e=>{const dot=document.createElement('div'); dot.style.cssText=`position:fixed;left:${e.clientX}px;top:${e.clientY}px;width:10px;height:10px;border-radius:50%;background:#00ff41;z-index:999999;pointer-events:none;`; document.body.appendChild(dot); setTimeout(()=>document.body.removeChild(dot),1000);}; document.addEventListener('mousemove',fn); setTimeout(()=>document.removeEventListener('mousemove',fn),10000); }
            else if (type === 'disco') { const c=['#f00','#0f0','#00f','#ff0','#f0f','#0ff']; let i=0; const iv=setInterval(()=>{document.body.style.background=c[i++%c.length];},200); setTimeout(()=>{clearInterval(iv); document.body.style.background='';},8000); }
            else if (type === 'gravity') { document.body.style.transition='transform 2s'; document.body.style.transform='translateY(100vh)'; setTimeout(()=>{document.body.style.transform=''; document.body.style.transition='';},3000); }
            else if (type === 'glitch') { styles.innerHTML='@keyframes glitch{0%,100%{transform:translate(0)} 20%{transform:translate(-5px,5px)} 40%{transform:translate(5px,-5px)} 60%{transform:translate(-5px,-5px)} 80%{transform:translate(5px,5px)}} body{animation:glitch 0.3s infinite}'; document.head.appendChild(styles); setTimeout(()=>document.head.removeChild(styles),5000); }
            else if (type === 'spin') { styles.innerHTML='@keyframes spin{0%{transform:rotate(0)} 100%{transform:rotate(360deg)}} body{animation:spin 2s infinite}'; document.head.appendChild(styles); setTimeout(()=>document.head.removeChild(styles),8000); }
            else if (type === 'blur') { document.body.style.filter='blur(10px)'; setTimeout(()=>{document.body.style.filter='';},6000); }
            else if (type === 'fake-update') { const d=document.createElement('div'); d.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:999999999;background:#0078d7;color:white;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;font-family:Segoe UI;'; d.innerHTML='<h1 style="font-size:80px;margin:0">35%</h1><p style="font-size:28px;margin-top:20px">Working on updates...</p>'; document.body.appendChild(d); setTimeout(()=>document.body.removeChild(d),8000); }
            else if (type === 'upside-down') { document.body.style.transform='scaleY(-1)'; setTimeout(()=>{document.body.style.transform='';},6000); }
            else if (type === 'backwards') { document.body.style.transform='scaleX(-1)'; setTimeout(()=>{document.body.style.transform='';},6000); }
            else if (type === 'invisible') { document.body.style.opacity='0.05'; setTimeout(()=>{document.body.style.opacity='';},5000); }
            else if (type === 'seizure') { const c=['#f00','#0f0','#00f','#ff0','#f0f','#0ff','#fff','#000']; let i=0; const iv=setInterval(()=>{document.body.style.background=c[i++%c.length]; document.body.style.filter=`invert(${i%2})`;},50); setTimeout(()=>{clearInterval(iv); document.body.style.background=''; document.body.style.filter='';},5000); }
            else if (type === 'fake-fbi') { const d=document.createElement('div'); d.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:999999999;background:#000;color:#fff;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;text-align:center;padding:40px;'; d.innerHTML='<h1 style="font-size:50px;color:red">🚨 FBI WARNING 🚨</h1><p style="font-size:24px">Illegal activity detected.</p><p style="font-size:20px">Your IP has been logged.</p>'; document.body.appendChild(d); setTimeout(()=>document.body.removeChild(d),7000); }
            else if (type === 'fake-crash') { const d=document.createElement('div'); d.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:999999999;background:#000;color:#fff;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-direction:column;font-family:monospace;'; d.innerHTML='<h1>FATAL ERROR</h1><p>Kernel panic — not syncing</p><p style="color:#888">0x000000ED (0x80F128D0)</p>'; document.body.appendChild(d); setTimeout(()=>document.body.removeChild(d),6000); }

            else if (type === 'tilt-fall') {
                let angle = 0;

                    angle += 2;
                    document.body.style.transform = 'rotate(' + angle + 'deg)';

                    if (angle >= 90) {

                        setTimeout(() => {
                            document.body.style.transform = '';

            else if (type === 'fake-battery') {

                document.body.appendChild(overlay);
                setTimeout(() => { overlay.style.opacity = '0'; }, 100);
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if(d.parentNode) document.body.removeChild(d);
                    if(overlay.parentNode) document.body.removeChild(overlay);
                }, 8000);
            }
        }

        // ================================
        // CONFIG / SETTINGS
        // ================================
        window.toggleCfg = (key) => { cfg[key] = !cfg[key]; document.getElementById('chkEnable').innerText = cfg.enable ? '✓' : ''; };
        window.toggleModal = (id) => { const m = document.getElementById(id); if(!m) return; m.style.display = m.style.display === 'block' ? 'none' : 'block'; };

        window.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (cfg.enable && (e.key === cfg.key || e.code === cfg.key)) panicTrigger();
            if (e.shiftKey && (e.key === 'L' || e.key === 'l')) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                const appVisible = document.getElementById('app').style.display === 'flex';
                if (!appVisible) document.getElementById('loginOverlay').style.display = 'flex';
                else toggleModal('updatesM');
            }
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                document.getElementById('panicOverlay').style.display = 'none';
                window.closeEmbedded?.();
            }
        }, true);

        // Add second listener without capture for better compatibility in iframes/embeds
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.shiftKey && (e.key === 'L' || e.key === 'l')) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                const appVisible = document.getElementById('app').style.display === 'flex';
                if (!appVisible) document.getElementById('loginOverlay').style.display = 'flex';
                else toggleModal('updatesM');
            }
        }, false);

        window.saveConfig = () => {
            cfg.url = document.getElementById('cfgUrl').value;
            cfg.key = tempKey;
            cfg.mode = document.getElementById('cfgMode').value;
            cfg.theme = document.getElementById('cfgTheme').value;
            cfg.cloak = document.getElementById('cfgCloak').value;
            cfg.panicMode = document.getElementById('panicMode').value;
            cfg.proxyUrl = (document.getElementById('cfgProxyUrl')?.value || '').trim();
            cfg.proxyMode = document.getElementById('cfgProxyMode')?.value || 'off';
            localStorage.setItem('pUrl', cfg.url); localStorage.setItem('pKey', cfg.key);
            localStorage.setItem('pMode', cfg.mode); localStorage.setItem('pEnable', cfg.enable);
            localStorage.setItem('pTheme', cfg.theme); localStorage.setItem('pCloak', cfg.cloak);
            localStorage.setItem('pPanicMode', cfg.panicMode);
            localStorage.setItem('pProxyUrl', cfg.proxyUrl);
            localStorage.setItem('pProxyMode', cfg.proxyMode);
            applyTheme(cfg.theme); applyCloak(cfg.cloak);
            awardSecretAch('theme_changer');
            const proxyStatus = cfg.proxyMode !== 'off' && cfg.proxyUrl ? ' · Proxy ON 🔒' : '';
            showToast('✅ Settings saved!' + proxyStatus);
            toggleModal('settingsM');
        };

        // ================================
        // UPDATES
        // ================================
        async function fetchUpdates() {
            onValue(ref(db,'updates'), renderUpdatesFromSnapshot, {onlyOnce:true});
        }

        function renderUpdatesFromSnapshot(snap) {
            const el = document.getElementById('updatesList'); if (!el) return;
            if (!snap?.exists()) { el.innerHTML = '<div class="update-item">No updates yet.</div>'; return; }
            const items = [];
            snap.forEach(c => { const v = c.val()||{}; items.push({id:c.key, ...v}); });
            items.sort((a,b) => (b.created||'').localeCompare(a.created||''));
            el.innerHTML = items.map(it => {
                const t = it.created ? new Date(it.created).toLocaleString() : '?';
                return `<div class="update-item"><div>${escapeHtml(it.text||'')}</div><span class="update-time">${escapeHtml(it.author||'SYSTEM')} • ${t}</span></div>`;
            }).join('');
        }

        window.adminAddUpdate = () => {
            const text = document.getElementById('adminUpdateInp').value || '';
            if (!text.trim()) return;
            const author = isMongle ? 'MONGLE' : (isAdmin ? 'OVERSEER' : 'ADMIN');
            push(ref(db,'updates'), {text:text.trim(), author, created: new Date().toISOString()})
                .then(() => { document.getElementById('adminUpdateInp').value=''; showToast('Update posted!'); });
        };

        window.adminAddUpdateFromUpdates = () => {
            const text = document.getElementById('updateText').value || '';
            if (!text.trim()) return;
            const author = isMongle ? 'MONGLE' : 'ADMIN';
            push(ref(db,'updates'), {text:text.trim(), author, created:new Date().toISOString()})
                .then(()=>{ document.getElementById('updateText').value=''; fetchUpdates(); showToast('Posted!'); });
        };

        // ================================
        // UTILS
        // ================================
        function escapeHtml(s) {
            if (typeof s !== 'string') return s ?? '';
            return s.replace(/[&<>"']/g, c => ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c]));
        }

        function escapeAttr(s) {
            if (typeof s !== 'string') return '';
            return s.replace(/'/g, "\\'").replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
        }

        function showToast(msg, dur=2500) {
            const t = document.getElementById('toast');
            t.innerText = msg; t.classList.add('show');
            setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), dur);
        }

        window.openMongleAboutBlank = () => {
            const w = window.open('about:blank');
            if (!w) return alert('Popup blocked!');
            const html = `<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><title>MONGLE X</title></head><body style="margin:0;background:#000"><iframe src="${location.href}" style="border:none;width:100vw;height:100vh;" allow="fullscreen"></iframe></body></html>`;
            w.document.open(); w.document.write(html); w.document.close();
        };

        // ================================
        // GAME REQUESTS
        // ================================
        window.loadGameRequests = () => {
            const el = document.getElementById('gameRequestsList');
            if (!el) return;
            el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555;">Loading...</div>';
            get(ref(db, 'gameRequests')).then(snap => {
                if (!snap.exists()) { el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#333;">No requests yet.</div>'; return; }
                const items = [];
                snap.forEach(c => items.push({ key: c.key, ...c.val() }));
                items.sort((a,b) => (b.t||0) - (a.t||0));
                el.innerHTML = items.map(r => `
                    <div style="padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid #111;display:flex;gap:8px;align-items:flex-start;">
                        <div style="flex:1;">
                            <div style="color:#fff;font-weight:bold;">${escapeHtml(r.name||'?')}</div>
                            ${r.url ? `<div style="color:#00cfff;font-size:9px;">${escapeHtml(r.url)}</div>` : ''}
                            ${r.reason ? `<div style="color:#555;font-size:10px;">${escapeHtml(r.reason)}</div>` : ''}
                            <div style="color:#333;font-size:9px;">by ${escapeHtml(r.requestedBy||'?')} · ${r.t ? new Date(r.t).toLocaleDateString() : '?'}</div>
                        </div>
                        <button class="btn btn-dark" onclick="remove(ref(db,'gameRequests/${r.key}'));loadGameRequests();" style="font-size:9px;padding:2px 6px;flex-shrink:0;">✓</button>
                    </div>`).join('');
            });
        };

        // ================================
        // REQUEST GAME
        // ================================
        window.showRequestGame = () => toggleModal('requestGameM');

        window.submitGameRequest = () => {
            const name = document.getElementById('reqGameName')?.value.trim();
            const url = document.getElementById('reqGameUrl')?.value.trim();
            const reason = document.getElementById('reqGameReason')?.value.trim();
            const status = document.getElementById('reqGameStatus');
            if (!name) { if(status) status.innerText = '❌ Please enter a game name'; return; }
            push(ref(db, 'gameRequests'), {
                name, url: url || '', reason: reason || '',
                requestedBy: myName || '?',
                t: Date.now()
            });
            if (status) status.innerText = '✅ Request submitted! The admin will review it.';
            document.getElementById('reqGameName').value = '';
            document.getElementById('reqGameUrl').value = '';
            document.getElementById('reqGameReason').value = '';
            awardSecretAch('requested_game');
            setTimeout(() => { toggleModal('requestGameM'); if(status) status.innerText=''; }, 2000);
        };

        applyTheme(cfg.theme);
        applyCloak(cfg.cloak);
        document.getElementById('cfgUrl').value = cfg.url;
        document.getElementById('cfgKeyDisp').value = cfg.key.toUpperCase();
        document.getElementById('cfgMode').value = cfg.mode;
        document.getElementById('chkEnable').innerText = cfg.enable ? '✓' : '';
        document.getElementById('cfgTheme').value = cfg.theme;
        document.getElementById('cfgCloak').value = cfg.cloak;
        document.getElementById('panicMode').value = cfg.panicMode;
        if (document.getElementById('cfgProxyUrl')) document.getElementById('cfgProxyUrl').value = cfg.proxyUrl || '';
        if (document.getElementById('cfgProxyMode')) document.getElementById('cfgProxyMode').value = cfg.proxyMode || 'off';
        if (cfg.panicImage) { document.getElementById('panicImagePreview').innerHTML = `<img src="${cfg.panicImage}" style="max-width:100%; max-height:80px; border-radius:4px;">`; }
        updatePanicOptions();

        // ================================
        // MATRIX RAIN (lockdown screen)
        // ================================
        // Start immediately and ensure it works in all contexts
        (function initMatrix() {
            // Use setTimeout to ensure DOM is fully loaded
            const startMatrix = () => {
                const canvas = document.getElementById('matrixCanvas');
                if (!canvas) { setTimeout(startMatrix, 100); return; }

                const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
                if (!ctx) { setTimeout(startMatrix, 100); return; }

                function resize() {
                    canvas.width = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || 800;
                    canvas.height = window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight || 600;
                }
                resize();
                window.addEventListener('resize', resize);

                const chars = 'MONGLE01アイウエオカキクケコサシスセソタチツテトナニヌネノ';
                const fontSize = 13;
                let cols = Math.floor(canvas.width / fontSize);
                let drops = Array(cols).fill(1);

                function draw() {
                    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.05)';
                    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
                    ctx.fillStyle = '#00ff41';
                    ctx.font = fontSize + 'px monospace';
                    cols = Math.floor(canvas.width / fontSize);
                    if (drops.length < cols) drops = drops.concat(Array(cols - drops.length).fill(1));
                    for (let i = 0; i < cols; i++) {
                        const c = chars[Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length)];
                        ctx.fillStyle = Math.random() > 0.95 ? '#fff' : '#00ff41';
                        ctx.globalAlpha = Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5;
                        ctx.fillText(c, i * fontSize, drops[i] * fontSize);
                        if (drops[i] * fontSize > canvas.height && Math.random() > 0.975) drops[i] = 0;
                        drops[i]++;
                    }
                    ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
                }

                const rainInterval = setInterval(draw, 40);

                // Stop rain when lockdown hides
                const obs = new MutationObserver(() => {
                    const ld = document.getElementById('lockdown');
                    if (ld && ld.style.display === 'none') { clearInterval(rainInterval); obs.disconnect(); }
                });
                const ld = document.getElementById('lockdown');
                if (ld) obs.observe(ld, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['style'] });
            };

            // Start when DOM is ready
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', startMatrix);
            } else {
                startMatrix();
            }
        })();

        // Show online count on login screen
        onValue(ref(db, 'presence'), snap => {
            let c = 0; snap.forEach(() => c++);
            const el = document.getElementById('loginOnlineCount');
            if (el) el.innerText = c + ' online';
        });
    </script>
</body>
